        apCorner(AP_UI.SpamAllFrame, 6)

        AP_UI.SpamAllLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        AP_UI.SpamAllLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 120, 1, 0)
        AP_UI.SpamAllLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 0)
        AP_UI.SpamAllLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        AP_UI.SpamAllLabel.Text = "Spam All"
        AP_UI.SpamAllLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        AP_UI.SpamAllLabel.TextSize = 12
        AP_UI.SpamAllLabel.TextColor3 = AP_THEME.TextPrimary
        AP_UI.SpamAllLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        AP_UI.SpamAllLabel.Parent = AP_UI.SpamAllFrame

        AP_UI.NearBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        AP_UI.NearBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 58, 0, 26)
        AP_UI.NearBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -130, 0.5, -13)
        AP_UI.NearBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(59, 165, 255)
        AP_UI.NearBtn.Text = "NEAR"
        AP_UI.NearBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        AP_UI.NearBtn.TextSize = 11
        AP_UI.NearBtn.TextColor3 = AP_THEME.TextPrimary
        AP_UI.NearBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
        AP_UI.NearBtn.Parent = AP_UI.SpamAllFrame
        apCorner(AP_UI.NearBtn, 6)

        AP_UI.OwnBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        AP_UI.OwnBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 58, 0, 26)
        AP_UI.OwnBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -65, 0.5, -13)
        AP_UI.OwnBtn.BackgroundColor3 = AP_THEME.AccentOrange
        AP_UI.OwnBtn.Text = "OWN"
        AP_UI.OwnBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        AP_UI.OwnBtn.TextSize = 11
        AP_UI.OwnBtn.TextColor3 = AP_THEME.TextPrimary
        AP_UI.OwnBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
        AP_UI.OwnBtn.Parent = AP_UI.SpamAllFrame
        apCorner(AP_UI.OwnBtn, 6)

        -- Spam All NEAR event
        AP_UI.NearBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if not hrp then return end
            local fn = _G.runAdminCommand
            if not fn then ShowNotification("SPAM", "Admin not ready"); return end
            local cmds = {"balloon", "inverse", "jail", "jumpscare", "morph", "nightvision", "ragdoll", "rocket", "tiny"}
            local nearest, minD = nil, math.huge
            for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if p ~= LocalPlayer and p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local d = (hrp.Position - p.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                    if d < minD then minD = d; nearest = p end
                end
            end
            if not nearest then ShowNotification("SPAM", "No player nearby"); return end
            ShowNotification("SPAM NEAR", "Spamming " .. nearest.DisplayName)
            task.spawn(function()
                for _, cmd in ipairs(cmds) do pcall(function() fn(nearest, cmd) end); task.wait(0.15) end
            end)
        end)

        -- Spam All OWN event
        AP_UI.OwnBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if not hrp then return end
            local fn = _G.runAdminCommand
            if not fn then ShowNotification("SPAM", "Admin not ready"); return end
            local cmds = {"balloon", "inverse", "jail", "jumpscare", "morph", "nightvision", "ragdoll", "rocket", "tiny"}
            local Plots = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
            if not Plots then return end
            local nearestPlot, nearestDist = nil, math.huge
            for _, plot in ipairs(Plots:GetChildren()) do
                local sign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
                if sign then
                    local yb = sign:FindFirstChild("YourBase")
                    if not yb or not yb.Enabled then
                        local p = sign:IsA("BasePart") and sign.Position or (sign.PrimaryPart and sign.PrimaryPart.Position)
                        if not p then local pp = sign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart", true); p = pp and pp.Position end
                        if p then local d = (hrp.Position - p).Magnitude; if d < nearestDist then nearestDist = d; nearestPlot = plot end end
                    end
                end
            end
            if not nearestPlot then ShowNotification("SPAM OWN", "No base found"); return end
            local owner = nil
            pcall(function()
                local S = require(ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Packages"):WaitForChild("Synchronizer"))
                local ch = S:Get(nearestPlot.Name)
                if ch then
                    local o = ch:Get("Owner")
                    if typeof(o) == "Instance" and o:IsA("Player") then owner = o
                    elseif type(o) == "table" and o.Name then owner = Players:FindFirstChild(o.Name) end
                end
            end)
            if not owner or owner == LocalPlayer then ShowNotification("SPAM OWN", "Owner not found"); return end
            ShowNotification("SPAM OWN", "Spamming " .. owner.DisplayName)
            task.spawn(function()
                for _, cmd in ipairs(cmds) do pcall(function() fn(owner, cmd) end); task.wait(0.15) end
            end)
        end)

        -- ── Player List ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        AP_UI.listFrame = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
        AP_UI.listFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, -30, 1, -198)
        AP_UI.listFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 15, 0, 193)
        AP_UI.listFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        AP_UI.listFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
        AP_UI.listFrame.ScrollBarThickness = 4
        AP_UI.listFrame.ScrollBarImageColor3 = AP_THEME.AccentPurple
        AP_UI.listFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        AP_UI.listFrame.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
        AP_UI.listFrame.Parent = AP_UI.frame

        AP_UI.layout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
        AP_UI.layout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
        AP_UI.layout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 8)
        AP_UI.layout.Parent = AP_UI.listFrame

        -- ── Create Player Card ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
        local function createPlayerRow(plr, isOwnerSlot, slotNum)
            local CARD_UI = {}
            CARD_UI.card = Instance.new("Frame")
            CARD_UI.card.Name = plr and plr.Name or ("Slot" .. (slotNum or 0))
            CARD_UI.card.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 70)
            CARD_UI.card.BackgroundColor3 = AP_THEME.CardBg
            CARD_UI.card.LayoutOrder = isOwnerSlot and 0 or slotNum or 1
            CARD_UI.card.Parent = AP_UI.listFrame
            apCorner(CARD_UI.card, 6)

            -- Info container (criado sempre, com ou sem player)
            CARD_UI.info = Instance.new("Frame")
            CARD_UI.info.Size = UDim2.new(0, 130, 1, 0)
            CARD_UI.info.Position = UDim2.new(0, plr and 40 or 8, 0, 0)
            CARD_UI.info.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            CARD_UI.info.Parent = CARD_UI.card

            CARD_UI.nameLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            CARD_UI.nameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 14)
            CARD_UI.nameLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 9)
            CARD_UI.nameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            CARD_UI.nameLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            CARD_UI.nameLabel.TextSize = 12
            CARD_UI.nameLabel.TextColor3 = AP_THEME.TextPrimary
            CARD_UI.nameLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            CARD_UI.nameLabel.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
            CARD_UI.nameLabel.Parent = CARD_UI.info

            CARD_UI.usernameLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            CARD_UI.usernameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 11)
            CARD_UI.usernameLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 23)
            CARD_UI.usernameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            CARD_UI.usernameLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
            CARD_UI.usernameLabel.TextSize = 10
            CARD_UI.usernameLabel.TextColor3 = AP_THEME.TextMuted
            CARD_UI.usernameLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            CARD_UI.usernameLabel.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
            CARD_UI.usernameLabel.Parent = CARD_UI.info

            -- Preenche nome/username (ou empty slot)
            if plr then
                CARD_UI.nameLabel.Text = plr.DisplayName
                CARD_UI.usernameLabel.Text = "@" .. plr.Name
                PlayerFramesAP[plr] = CARD_UI.card
            else
                CARD_UI.nameLabel.Text = isOwnerSlot and "Owner Slot" or ("Slot " .. (slotNum or 0))
                CARD_UI.usernameLabel.Text = "Empty"
                CARD_UI.usernameLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 100, 100)
                CARD_UI.card.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
                return CARD_UI.card -- Empty slot, retorna sem botões
            end

            -- ══ Daqui pra baixo só roda se plr existe ══

            -- L badge
            CARD_UI.lBadge = Instance.new("TextButton")
            CARD_UI.lBadge.Size = UDim2.new(0, 24, 0, 52)
            CARD_UI.lBadge.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0.5, -26)
            CARD_UI.lBadge.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 50, 50)
            CARD_UI.lBadge.Text = "L"
            CARD_UI.lBadge.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            CARD_UI.lBadge.TextSize = 16
            CARD_UI.lBadge.TextColor3 = AP_THEME.TextPrimary
            CARD_UI.lBadge.AutoButtonColor = false
            CARD_UI.lBadge.Parent = CARD_UI.card
            apCorner(CARD_UI.lBadge, 4)
            CARD_UI.lBadge.MouseEnter:Connect(function() apTween(CARD_UI.lBadge, {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 70, 70)}) end)
            CARD_UI.lBadge.MouseLeave:Connect(function() apTween(CARD_UI.lBadge, {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 50, 50)}) end)

            -- Fire ALL commands
            local allCmds = {"balloon", "inverse", "jail", "jumpscare", "morph", "nightvision", "ragdoll", "rocket", "tiny"}
            local function fireAllCmds()
                local fn = _G.runAdminCommand
                if not fn then ShowNotification("ADMIN", "Admin not ready"); return end
                ShowNotification("ADMIN", "Spamming ALL on " .. plr.DisplayName)
                task.spawn(function()
                    for _, cmd in ipairs(allCmds) do
                        if not (isOnCooldown and isOnCooldown(cmd)) then
                            pcall(function() fn(plr, cmd) end)
                            if _G.activeCooldowns then _G.activeCooldowns[cmd] = tick() end
                            if _G.setGlobalVisualCooldown then _G.setGlobalVisualCooldown(cmd) end
                        end
                        task.wait(0.15)
                    end
                end)
            end

            -- L badge click (laser)
            CARD_UI.lBadge.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                apTween(CARD_UI.lBadge, {BackgroundTransparency = 0.5}, 0.1)
                task.spawn(function()
                    useLaserCapeOnPlayer(plr)
                end)
                task.wait(0.1)
                apTween(CARD_UI.lBadge, {BackgroundTransparency = 0}, 0.1)
            end)

            -- Background button → clicking empty card area fires all
            CARD_UI.bgBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
            CARD_UI.bgBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
            CARD_UI.bgBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            CARD_UI.bgBtn.Text = ""
            CARD_UI.bgBtn.ZIndex = 0
            CARD_UI.bgBtn.Parent = CARD_UI.card
            CARD_UI.bgBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(fireAllCmds)

            -- Base Owner label (azul, estilo YWS)
            CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 11)
            CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 36)
            CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.Text = "Base Owner"
            CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.TextSize = 10
            CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(59, 165, 255)
            CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.Visible = false
            CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.Parent = CARD_UI.info

            CARD_UI.stealLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            CARD_UI.stealLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 11)
            CARD_UI.stealLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 47)
            CARD_UI.stealLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            CARD_UI.stealLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            CARD_UI.stealLabel.TextSize = 10
            CARD_UI.stealLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 220, 60)
            CARD_UI.stealLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            CARD_UI.stealLabel.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
            CARD_UI.stealLabel.Visible = false
            CARD_UI.stealLabel.Text = ""
            CARD_UI.stealLabel.Parent = CARD_UI.info

            -- Buttons container
            CARD_UI.btnContainer = Instance.new("Frame")
            CARD_UI.btnContainer.Size = UDim2.new(0, 170, 1, -12)
            CARD_UI.btnContainer.Position = UDim2.new(1, -175, 0, 6)
            CARD_UI.btnContainer.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            CARD_UI.btnContainer.Parent = CARD_UI.card

            local mainBtnHeight = isOwnerSlot and 32 or 52
            CARD_UI.btnRow = Instance.new("Frame")
            CARD_UI.btnRow.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, mainBtnHeight)
            CARD_UI.btnRow.Position = isOwnerSlot and UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0) or UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, -26)
            CARD_UI.btnRow.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            CARD_UI.btnRow.Parent = CARD_UI.btnContainer
            CARD_UI.btnLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
            CARD_UI.btnLayout.FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal
            CARD_UI.btnLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 4)
            CARD_UI.btnLayout.Parent = CARD_UI.btnRow

            local btns = {
                {text = "JAIL", cmd = "jail",    color = AP_THEME.AccentRed,    size = UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, mainBtnHeight), row = "main"},
                {text = "RAG",  cmd = "ragdoll", color = AP_THEME.AccentPurple, size = UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, mainBtnHeight), row = "main"},
                {text = "RKT",  cmd = "rocket",  color = AP_THEME.AccentOrange, size = UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, mainBtnHeight), row = "main"},
                {text = "BUN",  cmd = "balloon", color = AP_THEME.AccentGreen,  size = UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, mainBtnHeight), row = "main"},
            }

            -- Extra row com I M T C para base owner (estilo YWS)
            local extraRow
            if isOwnerSlot then
                extraRow = Instance.new("Frame")
                extraRow.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 24)
                extraRow.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, mainBtnHeight + 2)
                extraRow.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                extraRow.Parent = CARD_UI.btnContainer
                local extraLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
                extraLayout.FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal
                extraLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 4)
                extraLayout.Parent = extraRow

                table.insert(btns, {text = "I", cmd = "inverse", color = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 255),   size = UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, 24), row = "extra"})
                table.insert(btns, {text = "M", cmd = "morph",   color = Color3.fromRGB(180, 0, 255),   size = UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, 24), row = "extra"})
                table.insert(btns, {text = "T", cmd = "tiny",    color = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100), size = UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, 24), row = "extra"})
                table.insert(btns, {text = "C", cmd = "control", color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0),   size = UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, 24), row = "extra"})
            end

            for _, def in ipairs(btns) do
                local parentRow = (def.row == "extra") and extraRow or CARD_UI.btnRow
                local btn = Instance.new("TextButton")
                btn.Size = def.size
                btn.BackgroundColor3 = def.color
                btn.Text = def.text
                btn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                btn.TextSize = (def.row == "extra") and 9 or 10
                btn.TextColor3 = AP_THEME.TextPrimary
                btn.AutoButtonColor = false
                btn.Parent = parentRow
                apCorner(btn, 4)
                btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    local cd = isOnCooldown and isOnCooldown(def.cmd)
                    if not cd then
                        local fn = _G.runAdminCommand
                        if fn then
                            fn(plr, def.cmd)
                            if _G.activeCooldowns then _G.activeCooldowns[def.cmd] = tick() end
                            if _G.setGlobalVisualCooldown then _G.setGlobalVisualCooldown(def.cmd) end
                        end
                        apTween(btn, {BackgroundTransparency = 0.5}, 0.1)
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        apTween(btn, {BackgroundTransparency = 0}, 0.1)
                    end
                end)
                btn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                    if not (isOnCooldown and isOnCooldown(def.cmd)) then
                        apTween(btn, {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(
                            math.min(255, def.color.R * 255 + 30),
                            math.min(255, def.color.G * 255 + 30),
                            math.min(255, def.color.B * 255 + 30))})
                    end
                end)
                btn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                    apTween(btn, {BackgroundColor3 = def.color})
                end)
                task.spawn(function()
                    while btn and btn.Parent do
                        local cd = isOnCooldown and isOnCooldown(def.cmd)
                        btn.BackgroundTransparency = cd and 0.6 or 0
                        btn.TextTransparency = cd and 0.5 or 0
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)
            end

            -- Stealing state colors
            local STEALING_BG = Color3.fromRGB(75, 22, 22)
            local STEALING_BG_HOVER = Color3.fromRGB(95, 30, 30)
            local NORMAL_BG = AP_THEME.CardBg
            local NORMAL_BG_HOVER = Color3.fromRGB(30, 35, 45)

            -- Card hover (respects stealing state)
            local isCurrentlyStealing = false
            CARD_UI.card.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                apTween(CARD_UI.card, {BackgroundColor3 = isCurrentlyStealing and STEALING_BG_HOVER or NORMAL_BG_HOVER}, 0.2)
            end)
            CARD_UI.card.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                apTween(CARD_UI.card, {BackgroundColor3 = isCurrentlyStealing and STEALING_BG or NORMAL_BG}, 0.2)
            end)

            -- Status updater (stealing + base owner)
            task.spawn(function()
                while CARD_UI.card and CARD_UI.card.Parent do
                    task.wait(0.5)
                    if not plr or not plr.Parent then
                        pcall(function() CARD_UI.card:Destroy() end)
                        PlayerFramesAP[plr] = nil
                        break
                    end
                    -- Base owner check
                    local isBaseOwner = (CurrentBaseOwner == plr)
                    if isBaseOwner then
                        CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.Text = "Base Owner"
                        CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.Visible = true
                    else
                        CARD_UI.baseOwnerLabel.Visible = false
                    end
                    -- Stealing check
                    local isStealing = plr:GetAttribute("Stealing")
                    if isStealing then
                        local idx = plr:GetAttribute("StealingIndex")
                        CARD_UI.stealLabel.Text = idx and ("Stealing: " .. idx) or "Stealing: ???"
                        CARD_UI.stealLabel.Visible = true
                        if not isCurrentlyStealing then
                            isCurrentlyStealing = true
                            apTween(CARD_UI.card, {BackgroundColor3 = STEALING_BG}, 0.2)
                        end
                    else
                        CARD_UI.stealLabel.Visible = false
                        if isCurrentlyStealing then
                            isCurrentlyStealing = false
                            apTween(CARD_UI.card, {BackgroundColor3 = NORMAL_BG}, 0.2)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)

            PlayerFramesAP[plr] = CARD_UI.card
            return CARD_UI.card
        end

        -- ── Refresh player list ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
        local function refreshAdminPanel()
            for _, child in ipairs(AP_UI.listFrame:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("Frame") then child:Destroy() end
            end
            PlayerFramesAP = {}

            CurrentBaseOwner = GetCurrentBaseOwner()

            -- Slot 1: Owner slot (base owner ou empty)
            if CurrentBaseOwner and CurrentBaseOwner ~= LocalPlayer then
                createPlayerRow(CurrentBaseOwner, true, 1)
            else
                createPlayerRow(nil, true, 1)
            end

            -- Slots 2-7: outros jogadores ou empty
            local activePlayers = {}
            for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if plr ~= LocalPlayer and plr ~= CurrentBaseOwner then
                    table.insert(activePlayers, plr)
                end
            end

            for i = 2, 7 do
                local plr = activePlayers[i - 1]
                if plr then
                    createPlayerRow(plr, false, i)
                else
                    createPlayerRow(nil, false, i)
                end
            end
        end

        refreshAdminPanel()

        Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function() task.wait(0.5); refreshAdminPanel() end)
        Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(plr) PlayerFramesAP[plr] = nil; task.wait(0.1); refreshAdminPanel() end)

        -- ── Periodic base owner refresh (estilo YWS) ─────────────────────────
        task.spawn(function()
            while task.wait(2) do
                local newOwner = GetCurrentBaseOwner()
                if newOwner ~= CurrentBaseOwner then
                    refreshAdminPanel()
                end
            end
        end)

        -- ── Hide if configured ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
        if Config.HideAdminPanel then adminGui.Enabled = false end

    end)

    -- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    -- CLICK COMMANDS PANEL (estilo YWS)
    -- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    do
        local CC = {} -- namespace local para não estourar registros
        CC.Enabled = false
        CC.Target = nil
        CC.Highlight = nil
        CC.CooldownLabels = {}
        CC.LeftIndex = 1
        CC.LeftCmds = {"ragdoll", "balloon", "rocket", "tiny", "jail"}

        local T = {
            Bg = Color3.fromRGB(10, 14, 24),
            Purple = Color3.fromRGB(180, 0, 255),
            White = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),
            Green = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100),
            Red = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100),
            TextSec = Color3.fromRGB(185, 193, 199),
            Divider = Color3.fromRGB(73, 80, 87),
            Border = Color3.fromRGB(52, 58, 64),
        }

        local gui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
        gui.Name = "ClickCommandsPanel"
        gui.ResetOnSpawn = false
        gui.DisplayOrder = 100
        pcall(function() gui.Parent = game:GetService("CoreGui") end)
        if not gui.Parent then pcall(function() gui.Parent = gethui() end) end
        if not gui.Parent then gui.Parent = PlayerGui end

        local panel = Instance.new("Frame", gui)
        panel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 360, 0, 220)
        local ccPos = Config.Positions.ClickCommands or {X=1, Y=1, OffX=-380, OffY=-240}
        panel.Position = UDim2.new(ccPos.X, ccPos.OffX or -380, ccPos.Y, ccPos.OffY or -240)
        panel.BackgroundColor3 = T.Bg
        panel.BackgroundTransparency = 0.1
        Instance.new("UICorner", panel).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 12)
        local pStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", panel)
        pStroke.Color = T.Purple; pStroke.Thickness = 2; pStroke.Transparency = 0.3

        -- Make draggable
        do
            local drag, start, pos
            panel.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
                if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                    drag = true; start = input.Position; pos = panel.Position
                    input.Changed:Connect(function()
                        if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                            drag = false
                            Config.Positions.ClickCommands = {
                                X = panel.Position.X.Scale, Y = panel.Position.Y.Scale,
                                OffX = panel.Position.X.Offset, OffY = panel.Position.Y.Offset
                            }
                            SaveConfig()
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end)
            UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
                if drag and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
                    local d = input.Position - start
                    panel.Position = UDim2.new(pos.X.Scale, pos.X.Offset + d.X, pos.Y.Scale, pos.Y.Offset + d.Y)
                end
            end)
        end

        -- Title
        local title = Instance.new("TextLabel", panel)
        title.Size = UDim2.new(0.45, 0, 0, 30); title.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10)
        title.BackgroundTransparency = 1; title.Text = "Click Commands"
        title.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; title.TextSize = 13; title.TextColor3 = T.White
        title.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        local tGrad = Instance.new("UIGradient", title)
        tGrad.Color = ColorSequence.new{ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, T.Purple), ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, T.White)}

        -- Click labels (left side)
        local clickInfo = {
            {y=45, label="Left Click", desc="Ragdoll → Balloon → Rocket → Tiny → Jail"},
            {y=85, label="Right Click", desc="Jail"},
            {y=125, label="Middle Click", desc="Inverse, Jumpscare, Morph"},
        }
        for _, info in ipairs(clickInfo) do
            local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", panel)
            lbl.Size = UDim2.new(0.45, -10, 0, 16); lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, info.y)
            lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1; lbl.Text = info.label
            lbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; lbl.TextSize = 11; lbl.TextColor3 = T.White
            lbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            local desc = Instance.new("TextLabel", panel)
            desc.Size = UDim2.new(0.45, -10, 0, 14); desc.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, info.y + 18)
            desc.BackgroundTransparency = 1; desc.Text = info.desc
            desc.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham; desc.TextSize = info.y == 125 and 9 or 10; desc.TextColor3 = T.TextSec
            desc.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        end

        -- Toggle button
        local toggleBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", panel)
        toggleBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0.45, -10, 0, 30); toggleBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 1, -40)
        toggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = T.Red; toggleBtn.Text = "Disabled"
        toggleBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; toggleBtn.TextSize = 11; toggleBtn.TextColor3 = T.White
        toggleBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
        Instance.new("UICorner", toggleBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

        -- Load saved state
        CC.Enabled = Config.ClickCommandsEnabled or false
        toggleBtn.Text = CC.Enabled and "Enabled" or "Disabled"
        toggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = CC.Enabled and T.Green or T.Red

        toggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            CC.Enabled = not CC.Enabled
            toggleBtn.Text = CC.Enabled and "Enabled" or "Disabled"
            toggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = CC.Enabled and T.Green or T.Red
            Config.ClickCommandsEnabled = CC.Enabled
            SaveConfig()
            if not CC.Enabled and CC.Highlight then
                CC.Highlight:Destroy(); CC.Highlight = nil; CC.Target = nil
            end
        end)

        -- Divider
        local div = Instance.new("Frame", panel)
        div.Size = UDim2.new(0, 1, 1, -20); div.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, 10)
        div.BackgroundColor3 = T.Divider; div.BorderSizePixel = 0

        -- Cooldowns title (right side)
        local coolTitle = Instance.new("TextLabel", panel)
        coolTitle.Size = UDim2.new(0.45, 0, 0, 30); coolTitle.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 10, 0, 10)
        coolTitle.BackgroundTransparency = 1; coolTitle.Text = "Cooldowns"
        coolTitle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; coolTitle.TextSize = 13; coolTitle.TextColor3 = T.White
        coolTitle.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        local cGrad = Instance.new("UIGradient", coolTitle)
        cGrad.Color = ColorSequence.new{ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, T.Purple), ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, T.White)}

        -- Cooldown items
        local coolCmds = {
            {Name="Rocket", Cmd="rocket"}, {Name="Ragdoll", Cmd="ragdoll"},
            {Name="Balloon", Cmd="balloon"}, {Name="Inverse", Cmd="inverse"},
            {Name="Jail", Cmd="jail"}, {Name="NightVision", Cmd="nightvision"},
            {Name="Tiny", Cmd="tiny"}, {Name="Morph", Cmd="morph"},
        }
        for i, cmd in ipairs(coolCmds) do
            local item = Instance.new("Frame", panel)
            item.Size = UDim2.new(0.45, -10, 0, 16); item.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 10, 0, 40 + (i-1)*18)
            item.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            local nm = Instance.new("TextLabel", item)
            nm.Size = UDim2.new(0.55, 0, 1, 0); nm.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            nm.Text = cmd.Name .. ":"; nm.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham; nm.TextSize = 10
            nm.TextColor3 = T.TextSec; nm.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            local st = Instance.new("TextLabel", item)
            st.Size = UDim2.new(0.45, 0, 1, 0); st.Position = UDim2.new(0.55, 0, 0, 0)
            st.BackgroundTransparency = 1; st.Text = "Ready"
            st.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; st.TextSize = 10; st.TextColor3 = T.Green
            st.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right
            CC.CooldownLabels[cmd.Cmd] = st
        end

        -- GetPlayerUnderMouse
        function CC.GetPlayerUnderMouse()
            local mouse = LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
            local cam = Workspace.CurrentCamera
            local unitRay = cam:ScreenPointToRay(mouse.X, mouse.Y)
            local params = RaycastParams.new()
            params.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude
            if LocalPlayer.Character then params.FilterDescendantsInstances = {LocalPlayer.Character} end
            local result = Workspace:Raycast(unitRay.Origin, unitRay.Direction * 1000, params)
            if result then
                local char = result.Instance:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
                if char and char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") then
                    local plr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(char)
                    if plr and plr ~= LocalPlayer then return plr, char end
                end
            end
            local closest, closestDist = nil, 50
            for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if plr ~= LocalPlayer and plr.Character then
                    local root = plr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if root then
                        local sp, onScreen = cam:WorldToScreenPoint(root.Position)
                        if onScreen then
                            local dist = (Vector2.new(sp.X, sp.Y) - Vector2.new(mouse.X, mouse.Y)).Magnitude
                            if dist < closestDist then closestDist = dist; closest = plr end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            return closest, closest and closest.Character
        end

        -- Highlight player under mouse
        RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
            if not CC.Enabled then return end
            local plr, char = CC.GetPlayerUnderMouse()
            if plr and char then
                if CC.Target ~= plr then
                    CC.Target = plr
                    if CC.Highlight then CC.Highlight:Destroy() end
                    local h = Instance.new("Highlight")
                    h.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 80); h.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
                    h.FillTransparency = 0.3; h.OutlineTransparency = 0
                    h.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode.AlwaysOnTop
                    h.Parent = char
                    CC.Highlight = h
                end
            else
                CC.Target = nil
                if CC.Highlight then CC.Highlight:Destroy(); CC.Highlight = nil end
            end
        end)

        -- Execute commands on click
        local function flashHighlight(color)
            if CC.Highlight then
                TweenService:Create(CC.Highlight, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {FillColor = color, OutlineColor = color}):Play()
                task.delay(0.5, function()
                    if CC.Highlight then
                        TweenService:Create(CC.Highlight, TweenInfo.new(0.4), {FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(255,80,80), OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(255,50,50)}):Play()
                    end
                end)
            end
        end

        local function execCmd(plr, cmd)
            if _G.isOnCooldown and _G.isOnCooldown(cmd) then return end
            if _G.runAdminCommand then _G.runAdminCommand(plr, cmd) end
        end

        UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gpe)
            if gpe then return end
            if not CC.Enabled or not CC.Target then return end

            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                local cmd = CC.LeftCmds[CC.LeftIndex]
                execCmd(CC.Target, cmd)
                CC.LeftIndex = CC.LeftIndex % #CC.LeftCmds + 1
                flashHighlight(Color3.fromRGB(50, 255, 50))

            elseif input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton2 then
                execCmd(CC.Target, "jail")
                flashHighlight(Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100))

            elseif input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton3 then
                execCmd(CC.Target, "inverse"); task.wait(0.05)
                execCmd(CC.Target, "jumpscare"); task.wait(0.05)
                execCmd(CC.Target, "morph")
                flashHighlight(Color3.fromRGB(100, 100, 255))
            end
        end)

        -- Update cooldown labels
        task.spawn(function()
            while true do
                for cmd, label in pairs(CC.CooldownLabels) do
                    if _G.isOnCooldown and _G.isOnCooldown(cmd) then
                        label.Text = "CD"; label.TextColor3 = T.Red
                    else
                        label.Text = "Ready"; label.TextColor3 = T.Green
                    end
                end
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
        end)
    end

    local function findFlyingCarpet()
        local map = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Map")
        if not map then return nil end
        local carpet = map:FindFirstChild("Carpet")
        if not carpet then return nil end
        if carpet:IsA("Model") then
            if carpet.PrimaryPart then return carpet.PrimaryPart end
            for _, c in ipairs(carpet:GetChildren()) do if c:IsA("BasePart") then return c end end
        elseif carpet:IsA("BasePart") then
            return carpet
        end
        return nil
    end

    local function findClaimModel(podium)
        if not podium or not podium.Parent then return nil end
        local claim = podium:FindFirstChild("Claim")
        if claim and claim:IsA("Model") then
            if claim.PrimaryPart then return claim.PrimaryPart end
            for _, c in ipairs(claim:GetChildren()) do if c:IsA("BasePart") then return c end end
        end
        return nil
    end

    local function getTargetPodiumAndSafePosition(animalData, fallbackPos)
        if not animalData or not animalData.plot then return nil, fallbackPos end
        local plots = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
        local plot = plots and plots:FindFirstChild(animalData.plot)
        local podiums = plot and plot:FindFirstChild("AnimalPodiums")
        if not podiums then return nil, fallbackPos end
        local safeName = (fallbackPos and fallbackPos.Y > 8.8) and "13" or "3"
        local safePod = podiums:FindFirstChild(safeName)
        local safeBase = safePod and safePod:FindFirstChild("Base")
        local safeSpawn = safeBase and safeBase:FindFirstChild("Spawn")
        return safePod, (safeSpawn and safeSpawn:IsA("BasePart") and safeSpawn.Position) or fallbackPos
    end

    local function playFullScreenFlash()
        local flashGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
        flashGui.Name = "AutoTPFlash"
        flashGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
        flashGui.DisplayOrder = 999999
        flashGui.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling
        flashGui.IgnoreGuiInset = true
        flashGui.Parent = PlayerGui

        local flashFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
        flashFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
        flashFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        flashFrame.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0, 0)
        flashFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
        flashFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        flashFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
        flashFrame.Parent = flashGui

        local tweenIn = TweenService:Create(flashFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.075, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear), {BackgroundTransparency = 0})
        local tweenOut = TweenService:Create(flashFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.125, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear), {BackgroundTransparency = 1})
        tweenIn:Play()
        tweenIn.Completed:Connect(function()
            tweenOut:Play()
            tweenOut.Completed:Connect(function()
                flashGui:Destroy()
            end)
        end)
    end

    local isTpMoving = State.isTpMoving

    _G._isTargetPlotUnlocked = function(plotName)
        local ok, res = pcall(function()
            local plots = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
            if not plots then return false end
            local targetPlot = plots:FindFirstChild(plotName)
            if not targetPlot then return false end
            local unlockFolder = targetPlot:FindFirstChild("Unlock")
            if not unlockFolder then return true end
            local unlockItems = {}
            for _, item in pairs(unlockFolder:GetChildren()) do
                local pos = nil
                if item:IsA("Model") then pcall(function() pos = item:GetPivot().Position end)
                elseif item:IsA("BasePart") then pos = item.Position end
                if pos then table.insert(unlockItems, {Object = item, Height = pos.Y}) end
            end
            table.sort(unlockItems, function(a, b) return a.Height < b.Height end)
            if #unlockItems == 0 then return true end
            local floor1Door = unlockItems[1].Object
            for _, desc in ipairs(floor1Door:GetDescendants()) do
                if desc:IsA("ProximityPrompt") and desc.Enabled then return false end
            end
            for _, child in ipairs(floor1Door:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("ProximityPrompt") and child.Enabled then return false end
            end
            return true
        end)
        return ok and res or false
    end

    local function waitForFps(targetFps, timeout)
        targetFps = targetFps or 75
        timeout   = timeout   or 2
        local deadline = tick() + timeout
        repeat
            local dt = RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
            if 1 / dt >= targetFps then return end
        until tick() >= deadline
    end

    local function runAutoSnipe()
        if State.isTpMoving then return end

        local targetPetData = nil
        if Config.AutoTPPriority then
            local bestEntry = nil
            local cache = SharedState.AllAnimalsCache
            if cache and type(cache) == "table" then
                for _, pName in ipairs(PRIORITY_LIST) do
                    local searchName = pName:lower()
                    for _, a in ipairs(cache) do
                        if a and a.name and a.name:lower() == searchName and a.owner ~= LocalPlayer.Name then
                            bestEntry = a; break
                        end
                    end
                    if bestEntry then break end
                end
                if not bestEntry then
                    for _, a in ipairs(cache) do
                        if a and a.owner ~= LocalPlayer.Name then bestEntry = a; break end
                    end
                end
            end
            if bestEntry then targetPetData = bestEntry
            else
                if not SharedState.SelectedPetData then return end
                targetPetData = SharedState.SelectedPetData.animalData
            end
        else
            if not SharedState.SelectedPetData then return end
            targetPetData = SharedState.SelectedPetData.animalData
        end
        if not targetPetData then return end

        local char = LocalPlayer.Character
        local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        local hum = char and char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
        if not hrp or not hum or hum.Health <= 0 then return end

        State.isTpMoving = true

        local function finishTeleport()
            State.isTpMoving = false
        end

        local targetPart = findAdorneeGlobal(targetPetData)
        if not targetPart then finishTeleport(); return end

        local exactPos = targetPart.Position
        local targetPodium, targetPosition = getTargetPodiumAndSafePosition(targetPetData, exactPos)
        local isSecondFloor = targetPosition.Y > 10
        local claimPart = findClaimModel(targetPodium)

        local directionToPet = targetPosition - hrp.Position
        if directionToPet.Magnitude > 0 then
            directionToPet = Vector3.new(directionToPet.X, 0, directionToPet.Z).Unit
        else
            directionToPet = Vector3.new(0, 0, -1)
        end

        local dirBehind
        if claimPart then
            local df = claimPart.Position - targetPosition
            if df.Magnitude > 0 then
                dirBehind = -Vector3.new(df.X, 0, df.Z).Unit
            else
                dirBehind = -directionToPet
            end
        else
            dirBehind = -directionToPet
        end

        local behindPos = targetPosition + (dirBehind * 7)
        local rpPre = RaycastParams.new()
        rpPre.FilterDescendantsInstances = {char}
        rpPre.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude
        local resPre = Workspace:Raycast(
            Vector3.new(behindPos.X, targetPosition.Y + 10, behindPos.Z),
            Vector3.new(0, -1000, 0),
            rpPre
        )
        if not resPre then finishTeleport(); return end
        local finalHeight = resPre.Position.Y + 5.5
        local finalPos = Vector3.new(behindPos.X, finalHeight, behindPos.Z)
        local lookTarget = claimPart and Vector3.new(claimPart.Position.X, finalPos.Y, claimPart.Position.Z) or targetPosition

        local finalFacing = CFrame.lookAt(finalPos, lookTarget)
        local facingRot = finalFacing - finalFacing.Position
        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(hrp.Position) * facingRot

        if hrp.Position.Y > 25 and targetPosition.Y > 25 then
            hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
            hrp.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(finalPos) * facingRot
            hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
            hrp.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
        else
            local carpetName = Config.TpSettings.Tool or "Flying Carpet"
            local carpet = LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild(carpetName) or char:FindFirstChild(carpetName)
            if carpet and hum and hum.Parent then
                hum:EquipTool(carpet)
            end

            if not char.Parent or not hrp.Parent then finishTeleport(); return end

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(hrp.Position) * facingRot
            if hum and hum.Parent then
                hum:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
            end
            task.wait(0.01)
            if not char.Parent or not hrp.Parent then finishTeleport(); return end
            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(hrp.Position.X, 35, hrp.Position.Z) * facingRot
            task.wait(0.1)

            if not char.Parent or not hrp.Parent then finishTeleport(); return end

            local positionBehindPet = targetPosition + (dirBehind * 18)
            local carpetPart = findFlyingCarpet()
            if not carpetPart then finishTeleport(); return end

            if not char.Parent or not hrp.Parent then finishTeleport(); return end
            local carpetPos = carpetPart.Position
            local carpetPosAtHeight = Vector3.new(carpetPos.X, hrp.Position.Y, positionBehindPet.Z)
            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(carpetPosAtHeight) * facingRot
            task.wait(0.2)

            if not char.Parent or not hrp.Parent then finishTeleport(); return end

            hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
            hrp.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(finalPos) * facingRot
            hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
            hrp.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
        end

        task.wait(0.3)
        instantClone()
        while _G.isCloning do task.wait() end

    instantClone()
        while _G.isCloning do task.wait() end

        -- Equip Witch's Broom after cloning into base
        pcall(function()
            local broomChar = LocalPlayer.Character
            local broomHum = broomChar and broomChar:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if broomHum then
                local broom =
                    LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Witch's Broom")
                    or broomChar:FindFirstChild("Witch's Broom")
                if broom then
                    broomHum:EquipTool(broom)
                end
            end
        end)


        -- Xi TP: kicks in right after the clone TP lands
        task.wait(0.15)
        do
            local xiChar = LocalPlayer.Character
            local xiHrp = xiChar and xiChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            local xiTargetPart = findAdorneeGlobal(targetPetData)
            if xiHrp and xiTargetPart then
                local verticalDiff = xiTargetPart.Position.Y - xiHrp.Position.Y
                if verticalDiff > 2 then
                    local airPos = Vector3.new(xiTargetPart.Position.X, xiTargetPart.Position.Y - 8, xiTargetPart.Position.Z)
                    local plat = Instance.new("Part")
                    plat.Name = "XiTempPlatform"
                    plat.Size = Vector3.new(3, 1, 3)
                    plat.Position = airPos - Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)
                    plat.Anchored = true
                    plat.CanCollide = true
                    plat.Transparency = 0.3
                    plat.Parent = Workspace
                    RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
                    for i = 1, 10 do
                        if not LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Stealing") then
                            xiHrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(xiHrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity.X, 0, xiHrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Z)
                            xiHrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(airPos)
                            task.wait(0.05)
                        end
                    end
                    task.spawn(function()
                        local start = tick()
                        while tick() - start < 20 do
                            if LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Stealing") then break end
                            task.wait(0.1)
                        end
                        plat:Destroy()
                    end)
                else
                    for i = 1, 10 do
                        if LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Stealing") then break end
                        xiHrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(xiHrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity.X, 0, xiHrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Z)
                        if (xiHrp.Position - xiTargetPart.Position).Magnitude > 3 then
                            xiHrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(xiTargetPart.Position)
                            task.wait(0.05)
                        end
                        task.wait(0.05)
                    end
                end
            end
        end


        finishTeleport()
    end

    ;(function()
        local function isInsideStealHitbox()
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            if not char then return false end
            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if not hrp then return false end

            local petData = SharedState.SelectedPetData
            if not petData then return false end
            local animalData = petData.animalData or petData
            if not animalData or not animalData.plot then return false end

            local Plots = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
            if not Plots then return false end
            local plot = Plots:FindFirstChild(animalData.plot)
            if not plot then return false end

            local stealHitbox = plot:FindFirstChild("StealHitbox")
            if not stealHitbox then return false end

            local playerPos = hrp.Position

            local function checkPart(part)
                local cf = part.CFrame
                local sz = part.Size
                local lp = cf:PointToObjectSpace(playerPos)
                return math.abs(lp.X) <= sz.X/2
                and math.abs(lp.Y) <= sz.Y/2
                and math.abs(lp.Z) <= sz.Z/2
            end

            if stealHitbox:IsA("BasePart") then
                return checkPart(stealHitbox)
            elseif stealHitbox:IsA("Model") then
                for _, part in ipairs(stealHitbox:GetDescendants()) do
                    if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.Transparency < 1 then
                        if checkPart(part) then return true end
                    end
                end
            end
            return false
        end

        local _autoBackThread = nil
        local _autoBackStealConn = nil
        local _teleportingBelow = false
        local _forceAutoBackInstantCount = 0

        local function stopAutoBack()
            if _autoBackThread then task.cancel(_autoBackThread); _autoBackThread = nil end
            if _autoBackStealConn then _autoBackStealConn:Disconnect(); _autoBackStealConn = nil end
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if hrp then
                local bp = hrp:FindFirstChild("TP_BodyPosition")
                if bp then bp:Destroy() end
            end
            _teleportingBelow = false
        end

        local function getAutoBackTarget()
            local petData = SharedState.SelectedPetData
            if not petData then return nil end
            local animalData = petData.animalData or petData
            local part = findAdorneeGlobal(animalData)
            if not part then return nil end
            return part.Position, animalData
        end

        local function teleportBelowPet()
            if _teleportingBelow then return end
            _teleportingBelow = true
            pcall(function()
                local targetPos, animalData = getAutoBackTarget()
                if not targetPos then return end

                local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                if not char then return end
                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                local hum = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                if not hrp or not hum then return end

                local petX, petY, petZ = targetPos.X, targetPos.Y, targetPos.Z
                local playerY = hrp.Position.Y

                if playerY > 25 and petY > 25 then
                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPos)
                    hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                    hrp.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
                    _teleportingBelow = false
                    return
                end

                if playerY >= 8.8 and petY < 8.8 then return end
                if playerY <= 8.8 and petY > 24 then return end

                local carpetName = Config.TpSettings and Config.TpSettings.Tool or "Flying Carpet"
                local carpet = LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild(carpetName) or char:FindFirstChild(carpetName)
                if carpet and hum then hum:EquipTool(carpet); task.wait(0.1) end

                local targetY
                if petY > 22 or (playerY < 8.8 and petY >= 8.8) then
                    targetY = petY - 7.5
                else
                    local rp = RaycastParams.new()
                    rp.FilterDescendantsInstances = {char}
                    rp.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude
                    local res = Workspace:Raycast(Vector3.new(petX, petY, petZ), Vector3.new(0, -200, 0), rp)
                    targetY = res and (res.Position.Y + 1.4) or 0.5
                end

                local tPos = Vector3.new(petX, targetY, petZ)
                local dist = (Vector3.new(hrp.Position.X, targetY, hrp.Position.Z) - tPos).Magnitude

                if dist > 1.5 or math.abs(hrp.Position.Y - targetY) > 2 then
                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(petX, targetY, petZ)
                    hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                    hrp.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
                end

                local bp = hrp:FindFirstChild("TP_BodyPosition")
                if not bp then
                    bp = Instance.new("BodyPosition")
                    bp.Name = "TP_BodyPosition"
                    bp.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
                    bp.P = 10000
                    bp.D = 500
                    bp.Parent = hrp
                end
                bp.Position = tPos
                bp.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
            end)
            _teleportingBelow = false
        end

        local function startAutoBack()
            stopAutoBack()

            _autoBackStealConn = LocalPlayer:GetAttributeChangedSignal("Stealing"):Connect(function()
                if LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Stealing") == true then
                    local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                    local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if hrp then
                        local bp = hrp:FindFirstChild("TP_BodyPosition")
                        if bp then bp:Destroy() end
            task.spawn(function()
                    task.wait(0.1)
                            local rp = RaycastParams.new()
                            rp.FilterDescendantsInstances = {char}
                            rp.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude
                            local res = Workspace:Raycast(
                                Vector3.new(hrp.Position.X, hrp.Position.Y, hrp.Position.Z),
                                Vector3.new(0, -200, 0), rp
                            )
                            local floorY = res and (res.Position.Y + 1.4) or 0.5
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(hrp.Position.X, floorY, hrp.Position.Z)
                        end)
                    end
                end
            end)

            local lastTeleportTime = 0

            _autoBackThread = task.spawn(function()
                while Config.AutoBack do
                    pcall(function()
                        local stealing = LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Stealing")
                        local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                        local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if not hrp then return end

                        if stealing == true then
                            local bp = hrp:FindFirstChild("TP_BodyPosition")
                            if bp then bp:Destroy() end
                            return
                        end

                        local hasBP = hrp:FindFirstChild("TP_BodyPosition") ~= nil
                        local targetPos = getAutoBackTarget()
                        local inHitbox = isInsideStealHitbox()
                        local selected = SharedState.SelectedPetData
                        local selectedAnimal = selected and (selected.animalData or selected)
                        local targetPlotOpen = false
                        if selectedAnimal and selectedAnimal.plot and _G._isTargetPlotUnlocked then
                            targetPlotOpen = (_G._isTargetPlotUnlocked(selectedAnimal.plot) == true)
                        end

                        local forceInstantNow = (_forceAutoBackInstantCount or 0) > 0
                        local canAutoBackNow = forceInstantNow or (inHitbox and not targetPlotOpen)
                        if not hasBP and not _teleportingBelow and targetPos and canAutoBackNow then
                            local now = os.clock()
                            local delay = forceInstantNow and 0 or 0.05
                            if now - lastTeleportTime >= delay then
                                teleportBelowPet()
                                if forceInstantNow and _forceAutoBackInstantCount > 0 then
                                    _forceAutoBackInstantCount = _forceAutoBackInstantCount - 1
                                end
                                lastTeleportTime = now
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.01)
                end
                stopAutoBack()
            end)
        end

        if not Config.AutoBack then Config.AutoBack = false end

        _G.isInsideStealHitbox = isInsideStealHitbox
        _G.startAutoBack = startAutoBack
        _G.stopAutoBack = stopAutoBack
        _G.forceAutoBackInstant = function(times)
            _forceAutoBackInstantCount = math.max(tonumber(times) or 1, 1)
        end

        if Config.AutoBack then startAutoBack() end
    end)()

    -- ── Stage 3: Rest of GUIs (2s total delay) ──────────────────────────
    task.wait(1)

    local function executeReset()
        ShowNotification("RESET", "Reiniciando personagem...")
        local plr = LocalPlayer
        if not plr then return end

        task.spawn(function()
            pcall(function()
                local char = plr.Character
                if not char then return end

                local hum = char:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
                if hum then hum:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead) end

                char:ClearAllChildren()

                local dummy = Instance.new("Model")
                dummy.Parent = Workspace
                plr.Character = dummy
                plr.Character = char
                dummy:Destroy()
            end)
        end)
    end

    task.spawn(function()
        local function checkSteal(gui)
            if not Config.AutoKickOnSteal then return end
            local txt = (gui:IsA("TextLabel") or gui:IsA("TextButton")) and gui.Text
            if txt and string.find(txt, "You stole") then
                kickPlayer()
            end
        end
        PlayerGui.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(gui)
            checkSteal(gui)
            if gui:IsA("TextLabel") or gui:IsA("TextButton") then
                gui:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text"):Connect(function()
                    checkSteal(gui)
                end)
            end
        end)
        for _, gui in ipairs(PlayerGui:GetDescendants()) do
            checkSteal(gui)
        end
    end)

    UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, processed)
        if processed then return end
        
        local tpKey = safeKeyCode(Config.TpSettings.TpKey, Enum.KeyCode.T)
        local cloneKey = safeKeyCode(Config.TpSettings.CloneKey, Enum.KeyCode.V)
        local carpetKey = safeKeyCode(Config.TpSettings.CarpetSpeedKey, Enum.KeyCode.Q)
        local stealSpeedKey = safeKeyCode(Config.StealSpeedKey, Enum.KeyCode.Z)
        local resetKey = safeKeyCode(Config.ResetKey, Enum.KeyCode.X)
        local ragdollKey = safeKeyCode(Config.RagdollSelfKey, Enum.KeyCode.R)

        if input.KeyCode == tpKey then
            if _G._activePinConn then _G._activePinConn:Disconnect(); _G._activePinConn = nil end
            if _G._activePlat and _G._activePlat.Parent then _G._activePlat:Destroy(); _G._activePlat = nil end
            if _G.tpToBestBrainrot then pcall(_G.tpToBestBrainrot) else pcall(runAutoSnipe) end
        end

        if input.KeyCode == cloneKey then
            if _G._activePinConn then _G._activePinConn:Disconnect(); _G._activePinConn = nil end
            if _G._activePlat and _G._activePlat.Parent then _G._activePlat:Destroy(); _G._activePlat = nil end
            instantClone()
        end
        
        if input.KeyCode == carpetKey then
            carpetSpeedEnabled = not carpetSpeedEnabled
            setCarpetSpeed(carpetSpeedEnabled)
            if _carpetStatusLabel then
                _carpetStatusLabel.Text = carpetSpeedEnabled and "ON" or "OFF"
                _carpetStatusLabel.TextColor3 = carpetSpeedEnabled and Theme.Success or Theme.Error
            end
            ShowNotification("CARPET SPEED", carpetSpeedEnabled and ("ON  |  "..Config.TpSettings.Tool.."  |  140") or "OFF")
        end

        if input.KeyCode == stealSpeedKey then
            if SharedState.StealSpeedToggleFunc then
                SharedState.StealSpeedToggleFunc()
            end
        end

        if input.KeyCode == resetKey then
            executeReset()
        end
        
        if input.KeyCode == ragdollKey then
            task.spawn(function()
                if _G.runAdminCommand then
                    if _G.runAdminCommand(LocalPlayer, "ragdoll") then
                        ShowNotification("RAGDOLL SELF", "Triggered")
                    else
                        ShowNotification("RAGDOLL SELF", "Failed")
                    end
                else
                    ShowNotification("RAGDOLL SELF", "Function not available")
                end
            end)
        end

    end)

    local function CreateToggleSwitch(parent, initialState, callback)
        local sw = Instance.new("Frame")
        sw.Size = UDim2.new(0,40,0,20); sw.Position = UDim2.new(1,-50,0.5,-10)
        sw.BackgroundColor3 = initialState and Theme.Success or Theme.SurfaceHighlight
        Instance.new("UICorner", sw).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0); sw.Parent = parent
        local dot = Instance.new("Frame")
        dot.Size = UDim2.new(0,16,0,16)
        dot.Position = initialState and UDim2.new(1,-18,0.5,-8) or UDim2.new(0,2,0.5,-8)
        dot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255)
        Instance.new("UICorner", dot).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0); dot.Parent = sw
        local btn = Instance.new("TextButton"); btn.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
        btn.BackgroundTransparency = 1; btn.Text = ""; btn.Parent = sw
        local isOn = initialState
        local function SetState(s)
            isOn = s
            local tp = isOn and UDim2.new(1,-18,0.5,-8) or UDim2.new(0,2,0.5,-8)
            local tc = isOn and Theme.Success or Theme.SurfaceHighlight
            TweenService:Create(dot, TweenInfo.new(0.2,Enum.EasingStyle.Quad,Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Position=tp}):Play()
            TweenService:Create(sw,  TweenInfo.new(0.2,Enum.EasingStyle.Quad,Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {BackgroundColor3=tc}):Play()
        end
        btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() callback(not isOn, SetState) end)
        return {Set=SetState, Container=sw}
    end

    local rShowUnlockHUD = CreateRow("Show Unlock Buttons HUD")
    CreateToggleSwitch(rShowUnlockHUD, Config.ShowUnlockButtonsHUD, function(ns, set)
        set(ns); Config.ShowUnlockButtonsHUD = ns; SaveConfig()
        local hudGui = PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("BullysStatusHUD")
        if hudGui then
            local main = hudGui:FindFirstChild("Main")
            local unlockContainer = main and main:FindFirstChild("UnlockButtonsContainer")
            if main and unlockContainer then
                unlockContainer.Visible = ns
                if ns then
                    TweenService:Create(main, TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
                        Size = UDim2.new(0, 500, 0, 100)
                    }):Play()
                else
                    TweenService:Create(main, TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
                        Size = UDim2.new(0, 500, 0, 50)
                    }):Play()
                end
            end
        end
    end)
    CreateSectionHeader("ANTI-RAGDOLL")
    local arV1SetRef, arV2SetRef = {}, {}
    local rAr = CreateRow("V1")
    CreateToggleSwitch(rAr, Config.AntiRagdoll > 0, function(ns, set)
        arV1SetRef.fn = set
        if ns and Config.AntiRagdollV2 then
            set(false)
            ShowNotification("ANTI-RAGDOLL", "DISABLE V2 FIRST")
            return
        end
        set(ns)
        local mode = ns and 1 or 0
        Config.AntiRagdoll = mode
        if ns then
            Config.AntiRagdollV2 = false
            if arV2SetRef.fn then arV2SetRef.fn(false) end
        end
        SaveConfig()
        startAntiRagdoll(mode)
        if ns then startAntiRagdollV2(false) end
        ShowNotification("ANTI-RAGDOLL V1", ns and "ENABLED" or "DISABLED")
    end)
    local rArV2 = CreateRow("V2")
    CreateToggleSwitch(rArV2, Config.AntiRagdollV2, function(ns, set)
        arV2SetRef.fn = set
        if ns and Config.AntiRagdoll > 0 then
            set(false)
            ShowNotification("ANTI-RAGDOLL", "DISABLE V1 FIRST")
            return
        end
        set(ns)
        Config.AntiRagdollV2 = ns
        if ns then
            Config.AntiRagdoll = 0
            SaveConfig()
            if arV1SetRef.fn then arV1SetRef.fn(false) end
            startAntiRagdoll(0)
            startAntiRagdollV2(true)
        else
            SaveConfig()
            startAntiRagdollV2(false)
        end
        ShowNotification("ANTI-RAGDOLL V2", ns and "ENABLED" or "DISABLED")
    end)

        set(ns)

                if xrayEnabled and obj:IsA("BasePart") and obj.Anchored and isBaseWall(obj) then
                    originalTransparency[obj] = obj.LocalTransparencyModifier
                    obj.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0.95

            disableXray()

                autoTPPriorityToggleRef.setFn(true)
            end
        else
            local otherDefaults = Config.DefaultToHighest or Config.DefaultToPriority
            if not otherDefaults then
                set(true)
                ShowNotification("DEFAULT MODE", "At least one default must be enabled")
                return
            end
            Config.DefaultToNearest = false
            set(false)
        end
        SaveConfig()
        ShowNotification("DEFAULT TO NEAREST", ns and "ENABLED" or "DISABLED")
    end)

    CreateSectionHeader("CAMERA")
    local rFOV = CreateRow("FOV")
    local fovSliderBg = Instance.new("Frame", rFOV)
    fovSliderBg.Size = UDim2.new(0, 140, 0, 5)
    fovSliderBg.Position = UDim2.new(1, -200, 0.5, -2.5)
    fovSliderBg.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 32, 38)
    Instance.new("UICorner", fovSliderBg).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
    local fovFill = Instance.new("Frame", fovSliderBg)
    fovFill.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.Accent1
    fovFill.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0)
    Instance.new("UICorner", fovFill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
    local fovKnob = Instance.new("Frame", fovSliderBg)
    fovKnob.Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 12)
    fovKnob.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.TextPrimary
    fovKnob.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
    fovKnob.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, 0)
    Instance.new("UICorner", fovKnob).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
    local fovKnobStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", fovKnob)
    fovKnobStroke.Color = Theme.Accent1
    fovKnobStroke.Thickness = 1.5
    fovKnobStroke.Transparency = 0.2
    local fovValLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", rFOV)
    fovValLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0, 40, 0, 20)
    fovValLbl.Position = UDim2.new(1, -50, 0.5, -10)
    fovValLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    fovValLbl.Text = string.format("%.1f", Config.FOV)
    fovValLbl.TextColor3 = Theme.TextPrimary
    fovValLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    fovValLbl.TextSize = 13

    local function updateFOVSlider(val, skipSave)
        val = math.clamp(val, 30, 180)
        Config.FOV = val
        if not skipSave then SaveConfig(true) end
        fovValLbl.Text = string.format("%.1f", val)
        local pct = (val - 30) / 150
        fovFill.Size = UDim2.new(pct, 0, 1, 0)
        fovKnob.Position = UDim2.new(pct, 0, 0.5, 0)
        if Workspace.CurrentCamera then
            Workspace.CurrentCamera.FieldOfView = val
        end
    end
    updateFOVSlider(Config.FOV, true)

    local fovDragging = false
    fovSliderBg.InputBegan:Connect(function(i)
        if i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then fovDragging = true end
    end)
    UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(i)
        if i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then 
            if fovDragging then SaveConfig() end
            fovDragging = false 
        end
    end)
    UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(i)
        if fovDragging and (i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
            local x = i.Position.X
            local r = fovSliderBg.AbsolutePosition.X
            local w = fovSliderBg.AbsoluteSize.X
            local p = (x - r) / w
            updateFOVSlider(30 + (p * 150), true)
        end
    end)

        local rMenu = CreateRow("Menu Toggle Key")
        local bMenu = Instance.new("TextButton", rMenu)
        bMenu.Size=UDim2.new(0,80,0,24); bMenu.Position=UDim2.new(1,-90,0.5,-12)
        bMenu.BackgroundColor3=Theme.SurfaceHighlight; bMenu.Text=Config.MenuKey
        bMenu.Font=Enum.Font.GothamBold; bMenu.TextColor3=Theme.TextPrimary; bMenu.TextSize=12
        Instance.new("UICorner",bMenu).CornerRadius=UDim.new(0,4)
