            rowStroke.Color = td[3]
            rowStroke.Thickness = 1
            rowStroke.Transparency = 0.6

            local dot = Instance.new("Frame", row)
            dot.Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 12)
            dot.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0.5, -6)
            dot.BackgroundColor3 = td[3]
            dot.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Instance.new("UICorner", dot).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

            local nameLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", row)
            nameLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 1, 0)
            nameLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 32, 0, 0)
            nameLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            nameLbl.Text = td[1]
            nameLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            nameLbl.TextSize = 12
            nameLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 240, 240)
            nameLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

            local apBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", row)
            apBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 72, 0, 24)
            apBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -78, 0.5, -12)
            apBtn.BackgroundColor3 = td[3]
            apBtn.Text = "APPLY"
            apBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            apBtn.TextSize = 10
            apBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
            apBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
            Instance.new("UICorner", apBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

            local apStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", apBtn)
            apStroke.Color = td[3]
            apStroke.Thickness = 1
            apStroke.Transparency = 0.4

            local tid = td[2]
            apBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                applyTheme(tid)
                -- feedback visual
                local oldBg = tPanel.BackgroundColor3
                TweenService:Create(tPanel, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundColor3 = td[4]}):Play()
                task.delay(0.5, function()
                    TweenService:Create(tPanel, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {BackgroundColor3 = Theme.Background}):Play()
                end)
            end)
            apBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(apBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.25}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(rowStroke, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {Transparency = 0.1}):Play()
            end)
            apBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(apBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(rowStroke, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {Transparency = 0.6}):Play()
            end)
        end

        -- Botão de tema desativado - substituido pela nova UI
        local tToggle = Instance.new("TextButton", tGui)
        tToggle.Name = "ThemeToggleBtn"
        tToggle.Visible = false
        tToggle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 36, 0, 36)
        do
            local _st = Config.Positions and Config.Positions.ThemeToggle or {X = 0.01, Y = 0.01}
            tToggle.Position = UDim2.new(_st.X, 0, _st.Y, 0)
        end
        tToggle.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 20)
        tToggle.BackgroundTransparency = 0.1
        tToggle.Text = "🎨"
        tToggle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
        tToggle.TextSize = 18
        tToggle.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(185, 185, 185)
        tToggle.AutoButtonColor = false
        Instance.new("UICorner", tToggle).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
        local togStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", tToggle)
        togStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(170, 170, 170)
        togStroke.Thickness = 1.5
        togStroke.Transparency = 0.3
        MakeDraggable(tToggle, tToggle, "ThemeToggle")

        tToggle.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            tPanel.Visible = not tPanel.Visible
            if tPanel.Visible then
                tPanel.Position = UDim2.new(
                    tToggle.Position.X.Scale, tToggle.AbsolutePosition.X + 44,
                    tToggle.Position.Y.Scale, tToggle.AbsolutePosition.Y
                )
            end
        end)

        -- Pulso no botão toggle
        task.spawn(function()
            while tToggle.Parent do
                TweenService:Create(togStroke, TweenInfo.new(0.8, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut, -1, true), {Transparency = 0.7}):Play()
                task.wait(1.6)
            end
        end)

        -- Expor ref global para outros scripts
        _G.ThemeUI = {panel = tPanel, toggle = tToggle, apply = applyTheme}
    end)

    function buildBullysSettingsUI()
        local pg = PlayerGui
        if not pg then return end
        local oldBSG2 = pg:FindFirstChild("BullysSettings")
        if oldBSG2 then oldBSG2:Destroy() end

        local SUI = {}
        SUI.bsg = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
        SUI.bsg.Name = "BullysSettings"
        SUI.bsg.ResetOnSpawn = false
        SUI.bsg.IgnoreGuiInset = true
        SUI.bsg.DisplayOrder = 20
        SUI.bsg.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling
        SUI.bsg.Parent = pg

        -- ── cores base do tema ──
        local function C() return {
            BG   = Theme.Background,
            SURF = Theme.Surface,
            SH   = Theme.SurfaceHighlight,
            AC   = Theme.Accent1,
            TP   = Theme.TextPrimary,
            TS   = Theme.TextSecondary,
            ERR  = Theme.Error,
            SUC  = Theme.Success,
        } end

        -- Painel principal
        SUI.panel = Instance.new("Frame", SUI.bsg)
        SUI.panel.Name = "MainPanel"
        SUI.panel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 330, 0, 510)
        do
            local sp = Config.BullysSettingsPos
            if sp then
                SUI.panel.Position = UDim2.new(sp.X, 0, sp.Y, 0)
            else
                SUI.panel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 60, 0.5, -235)
            end
        end
        SUI.panel.BackgroundColor3 = C().BG
        SUI.panel.BackgroundTransparency = 0.31
        SUI.panel.BorderSizePixel = 0
        SUI.panel.Visible = false
        Instance.new("UICorner", SUI.panel).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)

        SUI.panStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", SUI.panel)
        SUI.panStroke.Color = Theme.Accent1
        SUI.panStroke.Thickness = 1.5
        SUI.panStroke.Transparency = 0.45
        task.defer(function() if addRacetrackBorder then addRacetrackBorder(SUI.panel, Theme.Accent1, 3) end end)

        -- Header
        SUI.hdr = Instance.new("Frame", SUI.panel)
        SUI.hdr.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 38)
        SUI.hdr.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        MakeDraggable(SUI.hdr, SUI.panel)
        -- Save position after drag ends
        SUI.hdr.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp)
            if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                inp.Changed:Connect(function()
                    if inp.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                        local ps = SUI.panel.Parent.AbsoluteSize
                        Config.BullysSettingsPos = {
                            X = SUI.panel.AbsolutePosition.X / ps.X,
                            Y = SUI.panel.AbsolutePosition.Y / ps.Y,
                        }
                        SaveConfig()
                    end
                end)
            end
        end)

        SUI.hTitle = Instance.new("TextLabel", SUI.hdr)
        SUI.hTitle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 120, 1, 0)
        SUI.hTitle.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
        SUI.hTitle.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        SUI.hTitle.Text = "BULLYS REMASTERED"
        SUI.hTitle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
        SUI.hTitle.TextSize = 16
        SUI.hTitle.TextColor3 = C().TP
        SUI.hTitle.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

        SUI.hFps = Instance.new("TextLabel", SUI.hdr)
        SUI.hFps.Size = UDim2.new(0, 150, 1, 0)
        SUI.hFps.Position = UDim2.new(0, 120, 0, 0)
        SUI.hFps.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        SUI.hFps.RichText = true
        SUI.hFps.Text = ""
        SUI.hFps.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        SUI.hFps.TextSize = 11
        SUI.hFps.TextColor3 = C().TS
        SUI.hFps.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        task.spawn(function()
            local fr, ac2 = 0, 0
            RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
                fr += 1; ac2 += dt
                if ac2 >= 1 then
                    local p2 = math.floor(LocalPlayer:GetNetworkPing()*1000)
                    local fc = fr>=50 and "rgb(80,255,150)" or "rgb(255,210,80)"
                    local pc = p2<100 and "rgb(80,255,150)" or "rgb(255,210,80)"
                    SUI.hFps.Text = string.format("<font color='%s'>FPS:%d</font>  <font color='%s'>PING:%dms</font>",fc,fr,pc,p2)
                    fr, ac2 = 0, 0
                end
            end)
        end)

        SUI.hClose = Instance.new("TextButton", SUI.hdr)
        SUI.hClose.Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20)
        SUI.hClose.Position = UDim2.new(1, -28, 0.5, -10)
        SUI.hClose.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        SUI.hClose.Text = "─"
        SUI.hClose.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        SUI.hClose.TextSize = 14
        SUI.hClose.TextColor3 = C().TS
        SUI.hClose.AutoButtonColor = false
        SUI.hClose.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() SUI.panel.Visible = false end)
        SUI.hClose.MouseEnter:Connect(function() SUI.hClose.TextColor3 = C().TP end)
        SUI.hClose.MouseLeave:Connect(function() SUI.hClose.TextColor3 = C().TS end)

        -- Divisor
        SUI.hDiv = Instance.new("Frame", SUI.panel)
        SUI.hDiv.Size = UDim2.new(1,-24,0,1)
        SUI.hDiv.Position = UDim2.new(0,12,0,38)
        SUI.hDiv.BackgroundColor3 = C().SH
        SUI.hDiv.BackgroundTransparency = 0
        SUI.hDiv.BorderSizePixel = 0

        -- Tab Bar (3 rows of 3)
        SUI.tabBar = Instance.new("Frame", SUI.panel)
        SUI.tabBar.Size = UDim2.new(1,-20,0,96)
        SUI.tabBar.Position = UDim2.new(0,10,0,44)
        SUI.tabBar.BackgroundTransparency = 1

        -- Content Area
        SUI.cArea = Instance.new("Frame", SUI.panel)
        SUI.cArea.Size = UDim2.new(1,-20,1,-148)
        SUI.cArea.Position = UDim2.new(0,10,0,148)
        SUI.cArea.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        SUI.cArea.ClipsDescendants = true

        -- ── helpers ──
        local function makeScroll()
            local sf = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame", SUI.cArea)
            sf.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
            sf.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            sf.BorderSizePixel = 0
            sf.ScrollBarThickness = 0
            sf.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Theme.Accent1
            sf.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,0)
            sf.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
            sf.Visible = false
            local ll = Instance.new("UIListLayout", sf)
            ll.Padding = UDim.new(0,5)
            ll.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
            local pp = Instance.new("UIPadding", sf)
            pp.PaddingTop  = UDim.new(0,5)
            pp.PaddingBottom = UDim.new(0,5)
            pp.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0,2)
            pp.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0,2)
            return sf
        end

        local function makeBtn(parent, lbl, order, callback)
            local btn = Instance.new("TextButton", parent)
            btn.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,38)
            btn.BackgroundColor3 = C().SURF
            btn.BackgroundTransparency = 0
            btn.Text = lbl
            btn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            btn.TextSize = 13
            btn.TextColor3 = C().TP
            btn.BorderSizePixel = 0
            btn.AutoButtonColor = false
            btn.LayoutOrder = order
            Instance.new("UICorner", btn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,7)
            local bs = Instance.new("UIStroke", btn)
            bs.Color = C().SH
            bs.Thickness = 1
            bs.Transparency = 0
            btn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(btn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3=C().SH}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(bs, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {Color=Theme.Accent1, Transparency=0.3}):Play()
            end)
            btn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(btn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3=C().SURF}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(bs, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {Color=C().SH, Transparency=0}):Play()
            end)
            btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(callback)
            return btn
        end

        local function makeSec(parent, lbl, order)
            local row = Instance.new("Frame", parent)
            row.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,22)
            row.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            row.LayoutOrder = order
            local bar = Instance.new("Frame", row)
            bar.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,1)
            bar.Position = UDim2.new(0,0,1,-1)
            bar.BackgroundColor3 = C().SH
            bar.BorderSizePixel = 0
            local tl = Instance.new("TextLabel", row)
            tl.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
            tl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            tl.Text = lbl
            tl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
            tl.TextSize = 11
            tl.TextColor3 = Theme.Accent1
            tl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            return row
        end

        local function makeToggle(parent, lbl, get, set, order)
            local row = Instance.new("Frame", parent)
            row.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,36)
            row.BackgroundColor3 = C().SURF
            row.BackgroundTransparency = 0
            row.BorderSizePixel = 0
            row.LayoutOrder = order
            Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,7)

            local tl = Instance.new("TextLabel", row)
            tl.Size = UDim2.new(1,-54,1,0)
            tl.Position = UDim2.new(0,10,0,0)
            tl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            tl.Text = lbl
            tl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            tl.TextSize = 12
            tl.TextColor3 = C().TP
            tl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

            local sw = Instance.new("Frame", row)
            sw.Size = UDim2.new(0,38,0,20)
            sw.Position = UDim2.new(1,-46,0.5,-10)
            sw.BackgroundColor3 = get() and Theme.Accent1 or C().SH
            Instance.new("UICorner", sw).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0)

            local dot = Instance.new("Frame", sw)
            dot.Size = UDim2.new(0,15,0,15)
            dot.Position = get() and UDim2.new(1,-17,0.5,-7.5) or UDim2.new(0,2,0.5,-7.5)
            dot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1,1,1)
            Instance.new("UICorner", dot).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0)

            local swb = Instance.new("TextButton", sw)
            swb.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
            swb.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            swb.Text = ""
            swb.ZIndex = 4; swb.AutoButtonColor = false
            local function doT()
                local ns=not get(); set(ns)
                TweenService:Create(dot,TweenInfo.new(0.15),{Position=ns and UDim2.new(1,-17,0.5,-7.5) or UDim2.new(0,2,0.5,-7.5)}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(sw,TweenInfo.new(0.15),{BackgroundColor3=ns and Theme.Accent1 or C().SH}):Play()
            end
            swb.MouseButton1Click:Connect(doT)
            swb.InputBegan:Connect(function(i) if i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.Touch then doT() end end)
            return row
        end

        local function makeKey(parent, lbl, get, set2, order)
            local row = Instance.new("Frame", parent)
            row.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,36)
            row.BackgroundColor3 = C().SURF
            row.BackgroundTransparency = 0
            row.BorderSizePixel = 0
            row.LayoutOrder = order
            Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,7)

            local tl = Instance.new("TextLabel", row)
            tl.Size = UDim2.new(1,-80,1,0)
            tl.Position = UDim2.new(0,10,0,0)
            tl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            tl.Text = lbl
            tl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            tl.TextSize = 12
            tl.TextColor3 = C().TP
            tl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

            local kb = Instance.new("TextButton", row)
            kb.Size = UDim2.new(0,64,0,24)
            kb.Position = UDim2.new(1,-72,0.5,-12)
            kb.BackgroundColor3 = C().SH
            kb.Text = get() or "NONE"
            kb.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            kb.TextSize = 11
            kb.TextColor3 = Theme.Accent1
            kb.AutoButtonColor = false
            Instance.new("UICorner", kb).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,5)
            kb.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                kb.Text = "..."; kb.TextColor3 = C().TS
                local con; con = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp)
                    if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then
                        set2(inp.KeyCode.Name)
                        kb.Text = inp.KeyCode.Name
                        kb.TextColor3 = Theme.Accent1
                        SaveConfig(); con:Disconnect()
                    end
                end)
            end)
            return row
        end

        -- ── TABS ──
        local TABS2 = {
            {name="Config",    id="cfg"},
            {name="Visuals",   id="vis"},
            {name="Movement",  id="mov"},
            {name="TP",        id="tp"},
            {name="UI Hide's", id="uih"},
            {name="Invis",     id="inv"},
            {name="Temas",     id="tem"},
            {name="BList",     id="bl"},
        }
        SUI.tBtns2 = {}
        SUI.tScrolls2 = {}
        SUI.activTab2 = "cfg"

        function SUI.switchTab2(id)
            if not SUI.tScrolls2[id] then id = "cfg" end
            SUI.activTab2 = id
            if _G.BullysSettingsUI then _G.BullysSettingsUI.currentTab = id end
            for tid, sc in pairs(SUI.tScrolls2) do sc.Visible = (tid==id) end
            for tid, tb in pairs(SUI.tBtns2) do
                local on = tid==id
                tb.BackgroundColor3 = on and Theme.Accent1 or C().SURF
                tb.BackgroundTransparency = 0
                tb.TextColor3 = on and Color3.new(0,0,0) or C().TS
                local s2 = tb:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIStroke")
                if s2 then s2.Transparency = on and 1 or 0.3 end
            end
        end

        do
            local COLS,BTN_H,GAP=4,28,4
            local rows = math.max(1, math.ceil(#TABS2 / COLS))
            SUI.tabBar.Size = UDim2.new(1,-20,0, rows * BTN_H + math.max(0, rows - 1) * GAP)
            SUI.cArea.Position = UDim2.new(0,10,0,44 + SUI.tabBar.Size.Y.Offset + 8)
            SUI.cArea.Size = UDim2.new(1,-20,1,-(SUI.cArea.Position.Y.Offset + 10))
            for i,td in ipairs(TABS2) do
                local col=(i-1)%COLS; local row=math.floor((i-1)/COLS)
                local tb=Instance.new("TextButton",SUI.tabBar)
                tb.Size=UDim2.new(1/COLS,-(GAP*(COLS-1)/COLS),0,BTN_H)
                tb.Position=UDim2.new(col/COLS,col==0 and 0 or GAP*(col/(COLS)),0,row*(BTN_H+GAP))
                tb.BackgroundColor3=C().SURF; tb.BackgroundTransparency=0
                tb.Text=td.name; tb.Font=Enum.Font.GothamBold; tb.TextSize=11
                tb.TextColor3=C().TS; tb.BorderSizePixel=0; tb.AutoButtonColor=false; tb.LayoutOrder=i
                Instance.new("UICorner",tb).CornerRadius=UDim.new(0,6)
                local ts2=Instance.new("UIStroke",tb); ts2.Color=C().SH; ts2.Thickness=1; ts2.Transparency=0.3
                SUI.tBtns2[td.id]=tb; SUI.tScrolls2[td.id]=makeScroll()
                local tid=td.id; tb.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() SUI.switchTab2(tid) end)
            end
        end

        -- ── CONFIG TAB ──
        SUI.cS = SUI.tScrolls2["cfg"]
        makeSec(SUI.cS, "AÇÕES RÁPIDAS", 0)
        makeBtn(SUI.cS, "Editar Priority List", 0, function()
            local priorityGui = PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("PriorityListGUI")
            if priorityGui then
                priorityGui.Enabled = not priorityGui.Enabled
                if priorityGui.Enabled and SharedState.RefreshPriorityGUI then
                    SharedState.RefreshPriorityGUI()
                end
            end
        end)
        makeBtn(SUI.cS, "Abrir Painel Admin", 1, function()
            local g = PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("XiAdminPanel")
            if g then g.Enabled = not g.Enabled end
        end)
        makeBtn(SUI.cS, "Auto Steal Painel", 2, function()
            local g = PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("AutoStealUI")
            if g then g.Enabled = not g.Enabled end
        end)
        makeToggle(SUI.cS, "Job Joiner", function()
            return Config.ShowJobJoiner
        end, function(v)
            Config.ShowJobJoiner = v
            SaveConfig()
            local g = PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("BullysJobJoiner")
            if g then g.Enabled = v end
        end, 3)

        -- ─── AUTO STEAL DEFAULTS ─────────────────────────────────────────────
        makeSec(SUI.cS, "AUTO STEAL DEFAULTS", 37)
        do
            SUI.rSwitches = {}
            local function applyDefMode(mode)
                Config.DefaultToNearest  = (mode == "nearest")
                Config.DefaultToHighest  = (mode == "highest")
                Config.DefaultToPriority = (mode == "priority")
                Config.DefaultToDisable  = (mode == "disable")
                Config.AutoTPPriority    = (mode == "nearest" or mode == "priority")
                SaveConfig()
                for _id, _sw in pairs(SUI.rSwitches) do
                    local _on = (_id=="nearest"  and Config.DefaultToNearest)
                            or (_id=="highest"  and Config.DefaultToHighest)
                            or (_id=="priority" and Config.DefaultToPriority)
                            or (_id=="disable"  and Config.DefaultToDisable)
                    TweenService:Create(_sw.dot, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {Position = _on and UDim2.new(1,-17,0.5,-7.5) or UDim2.new(0,2,0.5,-7.5)}):Play()
                    TweenService:Create(_sw.bg,  TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundColor3 = _on and Theme.Accent1 or Theme.SurfaceHighlight}):Play()
                end
            end
            local function makeRadioSwitch(parent, label, id, order)
                local isOn = (id=="nearest"  and Config.DefaultToNearest)
                        or (id=="highest"  and Config.DefaultToHighest)
                        or (id=="priority" and Config.DefaultToPriority)
                        or (id=="disable"  and Config.DefaultToDisable)
                local row = Instance.new("Frame", parent)
                row.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,36)
                row.BackgroundColor3 = C().SURF
                row.BackgroundTransparency = 0
                row.BorderSizePixel = 0
                row.LayoutOrder = order
                Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,7)
                local tl = Instance.new("TextLabel", row)
                tl.Size = UDim2.new(1,-54,1,0)
                tl.Position = UDim2.new(0,10,0,0)
                tl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                tl.Text = label
                tl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                tl.TextSize = 12
                tl.TextColor3 = C().TP
                tl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
                local sw = Instance.new("Frame", row)
                sw.Size = UDim2.new(0,38,0,20)
                sw.Position = UDim2.new(1,-46,0.5,-10)
                sw.BackgroundColor3 = isOn and Theme.Accent1 or Theme.SurfaceHighlight
                Instance.new("UICorner", sw).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0)
                local dot = Instance.new("Frame", sw)
                dot.Size = UDim2.new(0,15,0,15)
                dot.Position = isOn and UDim2.new(1,-17,0.5,-7.5) or UDim2.new(0,2,0.5,-7.5)
                dot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1,1,1)
                Instance.new("UICorner", dot).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0)

            rl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            rl.Text = "Rotation: "..Config.InvisStealAngle
            rl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            rl.TextSize = 12
            rl.TextColor3 = C().TP
            rl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            local rbg = Instance.new("Frame", r)
            rbg.Size = UDim2.new(1,-20,0,6)
            rbg.Position = UDim2.new(0,10,0,32)
            rbg.BackgroundColor3 = C().SH
            rbg.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Instance.new("UICorner", rbg).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0)
            local rfill = Instance.new("Frame", rbg)
            rfill.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.Accent1
            rfill.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Instance.new("UICorner", rfill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0)
            local rk = Instance.new("Frame", rbg)
            rk.Size = UDim2.new(0,13,0,13)
            rk.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5,0.5)
            rk.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1,1,1)
            rk.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Instance.new("UICorner", rk).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0)
            local function updRot(v)
                v = math.clamp(math.floor(v),180,360)
                Config.InvisStealAngle=v; _G.InvisStealAngle=v; SaveConfig()
                rl.Text = "Rotation: "..v
                local p2 = (v-180)/180
                rfill.Size = UDim2.new(p2,0,1,0)
                rk.Position = UDim2.new(p2,0,0.5,0)
            end
            updRot(Config.InvisStealAngle)
            local rd = false
            rbg.InputBegan:Connect(function(i)
                if i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                    rd=true; updRot(180+((i.Position.X-rbg.AbsolutePosition.X)/rbg.AbsoluteSize.X)*180)
                end
            end)
            UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(i)
                if i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.Touch then rd=false end
            end)
            UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(i)
                if rd and (i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
                    updRot(180+((i.Position.X-rbg.AbsolutePosition.X)/rbg.AbsoluteSize.X)*180)
                end
            end)
        end

        do  -- Depth slider
            local r = Instance.new("Frame", iS)
            r.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,52)
            r.BackgroundColor3 = C().SURF
            r.BorderSizePixel = 0
            r.LayoutOrder = 3
            Instance.new("UICorner", r).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,7)
            local rl = Instance.new("TextLabel", r)
            rl.Size = UDim2.new(1,-20,0,18)
            rl.Position = UDim2.new(0,10,0,4)
            rl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            rl.Text = "Depth: "..Config.SinkSliderValue
            rl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            rl.TextSize = 12
            rl.TextColor3 = C().TP
            rl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            local rbg = Instance.new("Frame", r)
            rbg.Size = UDim2.new(1,-20,0,6)
            rbg.Position = UDim2.new(0,10,0,32)
            rbg.BackgroundColor3 = C().SH
            rbg.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Instance.new("UICorner", rbg).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0)
            local rfill = Instance.new("Frame", rbg)
            rfill.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.Accent1
            rfill.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Instance.new("UICorner", rfill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0)
            local rk = Instance.new("Frame", rbg)
            rk.Size = UDim2.new(0,13,0,13)
            rk.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5,0.5)
            rk.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1,1,1)
            rk.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Instance.new("UICorner", rk).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0)
            local function updDepth(v)
                v = math.clamp(math.floor(v*10)/10, 0.5, 10)
                Config.SinkSliderValue=v; _G.SinkSliderValue=v; SaveConfig()
                rl.Text = "Depth: "..v
                local p2 = (v-0.5)/9.5
                rfill.Size = UDim2.new(p2,0,1,0)
                rk.Position = UDim2.new(p2,0,0.5,0)
            end
            updDepth(Config.SinkSliderValue)
            local dd = false
            rbg.InputBegan:Connect(function(i)
                if i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                    dd=true; updDepth(0.5+((i.Position.X-rbg.AbsolutePosition.X)/rbg.AbsoluteSize.X)*9.5)
                end
            end)
            UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(i)
                if i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.Touch then dd=false end
            end)
            UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(i)
                if dd and (i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or i.UserInputType==Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
                    updDepth(0.5+((i.Position.X-rbg.AbsolutePosition.X)/rbg.AbsoluteSize.X)*9.5)
                end
            end)
        end

        -- ── TEMAS TAB ──
        SUI.tS = SUI.tScrolls2["tem"]
        local tS = SUI.tS
        do
            local TDEFS2 = {
                {"Black",  "preto",    Color3.fromRGB(170,170,170)},

            for i2, td2 in ipairs(TDEFS2) do

                r.BorderSizePixel = 0
                r.LayoutOrder = i2
                Instance.new("UICorner", r).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,7)

                local dot2 = Instance.new("Frame", r)
                dot2.Size = UDim2.new(0,12,0,12)
                dot2.Position = UDim2.new(0,12,0.5,-6)
                dot2.BackgroundColor3 = td2[3]
                dot2.BorderSizePixel = 0
                Instance.new("UICorner", dot2).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0)

                local nl = Instance.new("TextLabel", r)
                nl.Size = UDim2.new(0.5,0,1,0)
                nl.Position = UDim2.new(0,32,0,0)
                nl.BackgroundTransparency = 1

                nl.TextColor3 = C().TP

                apb.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                apb.TextSize = 10
                apb.TextColor3 = isActive and Color3.new(0,0,0) or C().TP
                apb.AutoButtonColor = false

                apb.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    applyTheme(tid2)
                    -- atualiza visual de todos os botoes
                    for _, ch in ipairs(tS:GetChildren()) do
                        local b2 = ch:FindFirstChildOfClass("TextButton")
                        if b2 then
                            b2.BackgroundColor3 = C().SH
                            b2.Text = "APPLY"
                            b2.TextColor3 = C().TP
                        end
                    end
                    apb.BackgroundColor3 = tc2
                    apb.Text = "ACTIVE"
                    apb.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0,0,0)
                end)
            end
        end

        -- ── BLACKLIST TAB ──
        SUI.blS = SUI.tScrolls2["bl"]
        local blS = SUI.blS

        -- ESP config for blacklisted players
        makeSec(blS, "BLACKLIST ESP", 0)
        makeToggle(blS, "Show Blacklist ESP", function() return Config.BlacklistESP ~= false end, function(v)
            Config.BlacklistESP = v; SaveConfig()
            if not v then
                for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    local char = p.Character
                    if char then
                        local existing = char:FindFirstChild("BullysBlacklistESP")
                        if existing then existing:Destroy() end
                    end
                end
            end
        end, 1)

        -- Custom message row
        local blMsgRow = Instance.new("Frame", blS)
        blMsgRow.Size             = UDim2.new(1,0,0,36)
        blMsgRow.BackgroundColor3 = C().SURF
        blMsgRow.BackgroundTransparency = 0.05
        blMsgRow.BorderSizePixel  = 0
        blMsgRow.LayoutOrder      = 2
        Instance.new("UICorner", blMsgRow).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,7)
        local blMsgLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", blMsgRow)
        blMsgLbl.Size             = UDim2.new(0,60,1,0)
        blMsgLbl.Position         = UDim2.new(0,8,0,0)
        blMsgLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        blMsgLbl.Text             = "Mensagem"
        blMsgLbl.Font             = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        blMsgLbl.TextSize         = 11
        blMsgLbl.TextColor3       = C().TP
        blMsgLbl.TextXAlignment   = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        local blMsgBox = Instance.new("TextBox", blMsgRow)
        blMsgBox.Size             = UDim2.new(1,-78,0,24)
        blMsgBox.Position         = UDim2.new(0,72,0.5,-12)
        blMsgBox.BackgroundColor3 = C().SH
        blMsgBox.Text             = Config.BlacklistMsg or "BLOCKED"
        blMsgBox.PlaceholderText  = "BLOCKED"
        blMsgBox.Font             = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        blMsgBox.TextSize         = 11
        blMsgBox.TextColor3       = C().TP
        blMsgBox.ClearTextOnFocus = false
        blMsgBox.BorderSizePixel  = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", blMsgBox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,5)
        blMsgBox.FocusLost:Connect(function()
            local msg = blMsgBox.Text:gsub("%s+", " "):match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
            if msg == "" then msg = "BLOCKED" end
            Config.BlacklistMsg = msg; SaveConfig()
            blMsgBox.Text = msg
            -- Live-update all existing ESP labels
            for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                local char = p.Character
                if char then
                    local bb = char:FindFirstChild("BullysBlacklistESP")
                    if bb then
                        local lbl = bb:FindFirstChild("MsgLbl", true)
                        if lbl then lbl.Text = msg end
                    end
                end
            end
        end)

        -- Input row
        local blInputRow = Instance.new("Frame", blS)
        blInputRow.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,44)
        blInputRow.BackgroundColor3 = C().SURF
        blInputRow.BorderSizePixel = 0
        blInputRow.LayoutOrder = 1
        Instance.new("UICorner", blInputRow).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,7)

        local blBox = Instance.new("TextBox", blInputRow)
        blBox.Size = UDim2.new(1,-80,0,28)
        blBox.Position = UDim2.new(0,8,0.5,-14)
        blBox.BackgroundColor3 = C().SH
        blBox.Text = ""
        blBox.PlaceholderText = "Username..."
        blBox.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        blBox.TextSize = 12
        blBox.TextColor3 = C().TP
        blBox.ClearTextOnFocus = false
        blBox.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", blBox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,6)

        local blAddBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", blInputRow)
        blAddBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0,60,0,28)
        blAddBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1,-68,0.5,-14)
        blAddBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180,40,40)
        blAddBtn.Text = "ADD"
        blAddBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        blAddBtn.TextSize = 12
        blAddBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1,1,1)
        blAddBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
        blAddBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", blAddBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,6)

        -- Counter label
        local blCount = Instance.new("Frame", blS)
        blCount.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,24)
        blCount.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        blCount.LayoutOrder = 2
        local blCountLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", blCount)
        blCountLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
        blCountLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        blCountLbl.Text = "BLACKLISTED (0)"
        blCountLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
        blCountLbl.TextSize = 11
        blCountLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180,40,40)
        blCountLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

        -- List container
        local blListContainer = Instance.new("Frame", blS)
        blListContainer.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,10) -- auto grows
        blListContainer.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        blListContainer.LayoutOrder = 3
        blListContainer.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
        local blListLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout", blListContainer)
        blListLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0,4)
        blListLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder

        -- refreshBlacklistUI function
        refreshBlacklistUI = function()
            -- clear existing rows
            for _, ch in ipairs(blListContainer:GetChildren()) do
                if ch:IsA("Frame") then ch:Destroy() end
            end
            blCountLbl.Text = "BLACKLISTED (" .. #BlacklistedPlayers .. ")"

            for i, name in ipairs(BlacklistedPlayers) do
                local entRow = Instance.new("Frame", blListContainer)
                entRow.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,36)
                entRow.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50,20,20)
                entRow.BorderSizePixel = 0
                entRow.LayoutOrder = i
                Instance.new("UICorner", entRow).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,7)
                local entStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", entRow)
                entStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(180,40,40)
                entStroke.Thickness = 1; entStroke.Transparency = 0.5

                local iconLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", entRow)
                iconLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0,24,1,0)
                iconLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0,6,0,0)
                iconLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                iconLbl.Text = "🚫"
                iconLbl.TextSize = 14
                iconLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                iconLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255,100,100)

                local nameLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", entRow)
                nameLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1,-70,1,0)
                nameLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0,34,0,0)
                nameLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                nameLbl.Text = name
                nameLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                nameLbl.TextSize = 12
                nameLbl.TextColor3 = C().TP
                nameLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
                nameLbl.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd

                local remBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", entRow)
                remBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0,50,0,24)
                remBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1,-56,0.5,-12)
                remBtn.BackgroundColor3 = C().SH
                remBtn.Text = "❌"
                remBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                remBtn.TextSize = 13
                remBtn.TextColor3 = Theme.TextPrimary
                remBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
                remBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
                Instance.new("UICorner", remBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,6)
                local n = name
                remBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    pcall(function()
                        removeFromBlacklist(n)
                        ShowNotification("BLACKLIST", "✅ Removed: " .. n)
                        refreshBlacklistUI()
                    end)
                end)
            end

            if #BlacklistedPlayers == 0 then
                local empty = Instance.new("TextLabel", blListContainer)
                empty.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,36)
                empty.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                empty.Text = "No players blacklisted"
                empty.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
                empty.TextSize = 12
                empty.TextColor3 = C().TS
                empty.LayoutOrder = 1
            end
        end
        refreshBlacklistUI()

        blAddBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            pcall(function()
                local name = blBox.Text:gsub("%s", "")
                if name == "" then return end
                if addToBlacklist(name) then
                    ShowNotification("BLACKLIST", "🚫 Blocked: " .. name)
                    blBox.Text = ""
                    refreshBlacklistUI()
                else
                    ShowNotification("BLACKLIST", name .. " already blacklisted")
                end
            end)
        end)

        blBox.FocusLost:Connect(function(enter)
            if enter then blAddBtn.MouseButton1Click:Fire() end
        end)

        SUI.switchTab2("act")

        -- Expor ref global
        _G.BullysSettingsUI = {panel=SUI.panel, switchTab=SUI.switchTab2, currentTab="cfg"}
    end
    task.spawn(buildBullysSettingsUI)

    task.spawn(function()
        task.wait(1.5)
        if Config.CurrentTheme and THEMES and THEMES[Config.CurrentTheme] then
            applyTheme(Config.CurrentTheme)
        end
    end)

    -- ── AUTO PICKUP BRAINROT DA BASE (integrado ao botão Auto) ───────────────
    do
        local autoPickupActive = false
        local autoPickupKick   = false  -- kick após pegar o brainrot

        -- Função global para o botão Auto Kick (pickup) controlar
        _G.AutoPickupKickToggle = function(active)
            autoPickupKick = active
            Config.AutoPickupKick = active
        end

        local PICKUP_KEYWORDS = {"collect","coletar","pickup","pick up","pegar","grab","take"}

        local IGNORED_TOOLS_AP = {
            ["Flying Carpet"] = true,
            ["Quantum Cloner"] = true,
            ["Balloon"] = true,
        }

        local function ap_findMyPlot()
            local plots = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
            if not plots then return nil end
            local ok, Sync = pcall(function()
                return require(ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Packages"):WaitForChild("Synchronizer"))
            end)
            if not ok or not Sync then return nil end
            for _, plot in ipairs(plots:GetChildren()) do
                local okCh, ch = pcall(function() return Sync:Get(plot.Name) end)
                if okCh and ch then
                    local owner = ch:Get("Owner")
                    if owner then
                        local uid = (typeof(owner) == "Instance" and owner:IsA("Player") and owner.UserId)
                                 or (type(owner) == "table" and owner.UserId)
                        if uid == LocalPlayer.UserId then return plot end
                    end
                end
            end
            return nil
        end

        local function ap_isInsideMyBase(hrp, myPlot)
            if not hrp or not myPlot then return false end
            local sign = myPlot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
            if not sign then return false end
            local signPart = sign:IsA("BasePart") and sign
                          or sign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart", true)
            if not signPart then return false end
            local d = (Vector2.new(hrp.Position.X, hrp.Position.Z) - Vector2.new(signPart.Position.X, signPart.Position.Z)).Magnitude
            return d < 200
        end

        local function ap_isHoldingBrainrot()
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            if not char then return false end
            local carpetName = (Config.TpSettings and Config.TpSettings.Tool) or "Flying Carpet"
            for _, v in ipairs(char:GetChildren()) do
                if v:IsA("Tool") then
                    if v.Name == carpetName then continue end
                    if IGNORED_TOOLS_AP[v.Name] then continue end
                    return true
                end
            end
            return false
        end

        local function ap_getPromptForPart(animalData, myPlot)
            if not animalData or not myPlot then return nil end
            -- Busca dentro do podium ESPECÍFICO do brainrot (pelo slot),
            -- evitando pegar o prompt de um vizinho de menor gen
            local podiums = myPlot:FindFirstChild("AnimalPodiums")
            if not podiums then return nil end
            local podium = podiums:FindFirstChild(animalData.slot)
            if not podium then return nil end
            for _, obj in ipairs(podium:GetDescendants()) do
                if obj:IsA("ProximityPrompt") and obj.Enabled then
                    local txt = (obj.ActionText or ""):lower()
                    for _, kw in ipairs(PICKUP_KEYWORDS) do
                        if txt:find(kw) then return obj end
                    end
                end
            end
            return nil
        end

        local function ap_getBestBaseTarget()
            local cache = SharedState.AllAnimalsCache
            if not cache then return nil, nil end
            local myName = LocalPlayer.Name
            local bestPart, bestData = nil, nil
            local bestGv = -1
            for _, a in ipairs(cache) do
                if a and a.owner == myName and (tonumber(a.genValue) or 0) > bestGv then
                    local part = findAdorneeGlobal(a)
                    if part and part.Parent then
                        bestGv   = tonumber(a.genValue)
                        bestPart = part
                        bestData = a
                    end
                end
            end
            return bestPart, bestData
        end

        -- Função global para o botão Auto controlar o pickup
        _G.AutoPickupTitanzToggle = function(active)
            autoPickupActive = active
        end

        -- Variáveis compartilhadas entre o loop e o watcher de dano
        local lastTargetPart    = nil
        local kickWatcherActive = false

        -- Watcher de dano: se levar hit com brainrot na mao -> força re-pickup
        task.spawn(function()
            local onHitConn  = nil
            local lastHealth = math.huge

            local function connectHitListener()
                if onHitConn then onHitConn:Disconnect(); onHitConn = nil end
                local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                local hum  = char and char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                if not hum then return end
                lastHealth = hum.Health
                onHitConn = hum.HealthChanged:Connect(function(newHealth)
                    if not autoPickupActive then lastHealth = newHealth; return end
                    if newHealth < lastHealth and ap_isHoldingBrainrot() then
                        -- Levou dano com brainrot na mao: cancela kick e forca re-pickup
                        lastTargetPart    = nil
                        kickWatcherActive = false
                    end
                    lastHealth = newHealth
                end)
            end

            connectHitListener()
            LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
                task.wait(0.5)
                lastHealth = math.huge
                connectHitListener()
            end)
        end)

        -- Loop principal de pickup
        task.spawn(function()
            local myPlot           = nil
            local plotRefreshTimer = 0

            while true do
                task.wait(0.3)

                if not autoPickupActive then
                    lastTargetPart = nil
                    continue
                end

                local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                local hrp  = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if not hrp then continue end

                -- Atualiza o plot a cada 10s
                if not myPlot or (tick() - plotRefreshTimer) > 10 then
                    myPlot = ap_findMyPlot()
                    plotRefreshTimer = tick()
                end

                -- Só age dentro da própria base
                if not ap_isInsideMyBase(hrp, myPlot) then
                    lastTargetPart = nil
                    continue
                end

                -- Para se já está segurando um brainrot
                if ap_isHoldingBrainrot() then
                    lastTargetPart = nil
                    continue
                end

                -- Procura o brainrot com MAIOR gen da base
                local targetPart, targetData = ap_getBestBaseTarget()
                if not targetPart or not targetData then
                    lastTargetPart = nil
                    continue
                end

                -- TP somente se o target mudou (evita teleporte repetido a cada tick)
                if targetPart ~= lastTargetPart then
                    lastTargetPart = targetPart

                    -- 1) Equipa o carpet antes do TP para manter no ar
                    pcall(function()
                        local hum = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        if hum then
                            local carpetName = (Config.TpSettings and Config.TpSettings.Tool) or "Flying Carpet"
                            local carpet = LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild(carpetName)
                                        or char:FindFirstChild(carpetName)
                            if carpet then hum:EquipTool(carpet) end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.05)

                    -- 2) TP direto para cima do brainrot
                    pcall(function()
                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPart.Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.35) -- pausa maior para o servidor confirmar a posição
                end

                -- 3) Dispara o prompt do podium EXATO do brainrot de maior gen
                -- Tenta até 3 vezes com delay entre tentativas para garantir o pickup
                local prompt = ap_getPromptForPart(targetData, myPlot)
                if not prompt then continue end

                for attempt = 1, 3 do
                    if ap_isHoldingBrainrot() then break end -- já pegou, para
                    pcall(function()
                        if fireproximityprompt then
                            fireproximityprompt(prompt)
                        else
                            prompt:InputBegan(Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1)
                            task.wait(0.05)
                            prompt:InputEnded(Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1)
                        end
                    end)
                    if attempt < 3 then task.wait(0.15) end
                end

                -- 4) Watcher de kick: assim que o brainrot entrar na mão, kika
                -- (só um watcher ativo por vez para não acumular)
                if not kickWatcherActive then
                    kickWatcherActive = true
                    task.spawn(function()
                        local waited = 0
                        repeat
                            task.wait(0.1)
                            waited = waited + 0.1
                        until ap_isHoldingBrainrot() or waited >= 3
                        kickWatcherActive = false
                        if ap_isHoldingBrainrot() then
                            pcall(kickPlayer)
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end
        end)
    end
    -- ── FIM AUTO PICKUP BRAINROT ─────────────────────────────────────────────

    function buildMiniActionsUI()
        local pg = PlayerGui
        if not pg then return end
        local oldG = pg:FindFirstChild("BullysMiniActions")
        if oldG then oldG:Destroy() end

        local UI = {
            T = {
                Bg = Color3.fromRGB(15, 22, 28),
                BtnBg = Color3.fromRGB(12, 10, 18),
                FovRed = Color3.fromRGB(255, 90, 80),
                RotPurple = Color3.fromRGB(180, 50, 255),
                DepOrange = Color3.fromRGB(255, 110, 50),
                TextPrimary = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),
                TextOn = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100),
                TextOff = Color3.fromRGB(255, 90, 80),
            }
        }

        UI.maGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
        UI.maGui.Name = "BullysMiniActions"
        UI.maGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
        UI.maGui.IgnoreGuiInset = true
        UI.maGui.DisplayOrder = 25
        UI.maGui.Parent = pg

        UI.panel = Instance.new("Frame", UI.maGui)
        UI.panel.Name = "MiniPanel"
        UI.panel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 420, 0, 285)
        local savedPos = Config.Positions.MiniActions or {X=0.01, Y=0.35}
        UI.panel.Position = UDim2.new(savedPos.X, 0, savedPos.Y, 0)
        UI.panel.BackgroundColor3 = UI.T.Bg
        UI.panel.BackgroundTransparency = 0.15
        UI.panel.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", UI.panel).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
        UI.pStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", UI.panel)
        UI.pStroke.Color = Color3.new(0,0,0); UI.pStroke.Thickness = 1.5; UI.pStroke.Transparency = 0.5

        -- Dragging (Header invisível)
        UI.dragArea = Instance.new("Frame", UI.panel)
        UI.dragArea.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
        UI.dragArea.BackgroundTransparency = 1

        do
            local dragging, dragStart, startPos
            local conn1, conn2, conn3

            conn1 = UI.dragArea.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
                if Config.UILocked or _G.SliderDragging then return end
                if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                    dragging = true
                    dragStart = input.Position
                    startPos = UI.panel.Position
                end
            end)

            conn2 = UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
                if not (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then return end
                if not dragging then return end
                dragging = false
                -- Salva posição usando AbsolutePosition
                task.defer(function()
                    if not UI.panel or not UI.panel.Parent then return end
                    local screenSize = workspace.CurrentCamera and workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize or Vector2.new(1920, 1080)
                    if screenSize.X > 0 and screenSize.Y > 0 then
                        local sx = UI.panel.AbsolutePosition.X / screenSize.X
                        local sy = UI.panel.AbsolutePosition.Y / screenSize.Y
                        Config.Positions.MiniActions = {X = sx, Y = sy}
                        -- Normaliza a posição para Scale puro (sem offset acumulado)
                        UI.panel.Position = UDim2.new(sx, 0, sy, 0)
                        SaveConfig(true)
                    end
                end)
            end)

            conn3 = UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
                if not dragging then return end
                if not (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then return end
                local delta = input.Position - dragStart
                UI.panel.Position = UDim2.new(
                    startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + delta.X,
                    startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
                )
            end)

            -- Limpa conexões quando o painel for destruído
            UI.maGui.AncestryChanged:Connect(function()
                if not UI.maGui.Parent then
                    if conn1 then conn1:Disconnect() end
                    if conn2 then conn2:Disconnect() end
                    if conn3 then conn3:Disconnect() end
                end
            end)
        end

        -- Helper: UICorner
        local function addCorner(obj, r)
            local c = Instance.new("UICorner", obj); c.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, r or 6)
        end

        -- ── TOP ROW: FOV SLIDER ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
        UI.fovLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", UI.panel)
        UI.fovLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 20); UI.fovLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10)
        UI.fovLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1; UI.fovLabel.Text = "FOV"; UI.fovLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; UI.fovLabel.TextSize = 12; UI.fovLabel.TextColor3 = UI.T.FovRed

        UI.fovTrack = Instance.new("Frame", UI.panel)
        UI.fovTrack.Size = UDim2.new(0, 180, 0, 4); UI.fovTrack.Position = UDim2.new(0, 45, 0, 18); UI.fovTrack.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
        addCorner(UI.fovTrack, 2)

        UI.fovFill = Instance.new("Frame", UI.fovTrack)
        UI.fovFill.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 1, 0); UI.fovFill.BackgroundColor3 = UI.T.FovRed; addCorner(UI.fovFill, 2)

        UI.fovHandle = Instance.new("Frame", UI.fovTrack)
        UI.fovHandle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 12); UI.fovHandle.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -6, 0.5, -6); UI.fovHandle.BackgroundColor3 = UI.T.FovRed; addCorner(UI.fovHandle, 6)

        UI.fovVal = Instance.new("TextLabel", UI.panel)
        UI.fovVal.Size = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 20); UI.fovVal.Position = UDim2.new(0, 235, 0, 10)
        UI.fovVal.BackgroundTransparency = 1; UI.fovVal.Text = tostring(Config.FOV or 106); UI.fovVal.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; UI.fovVal.TextSize = 12; UI.fovVal.TextColor3 = UI.T.FovRed

        UI.fovReset = Instance.new("TextButton", UI.panel)
        UI.fovReset.Size = UDim2.new(0, 16, 0, 16); UI.fovReset.Position = UDim2.new(0, 260, 0, 12)
        UI.fovReset.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 20, 20); UI.fovReset.Text = "R"; UI.fovReset.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; UI.fovReset.TextSize = 10; UI.fovReset.TextColor3 = UI.T.FovRed; addCorner(UI.fovReset, 4)

        local fovMIN, fovMAX = 70, 120
        local function updFov(v, skipSave)
            v = math.clamp(math.floor(v), fovMIN, fovMAX)
            Config.FOV = v
            if not skipSave then SaveConfig(true) end
            UI.fovVal.Text = tostring(v)
            local pct = (v-fovMIN)/(fovMAX-fovMIN)
            UI.fovFill.Size = UDim2.new(pct, 0, 1, 0)
            UI.fovHandle.Position = UDim2.new(pct, -6, 0.5, -6)
            pcall(function() Workspace.CurrentCamera.FieldOfView = v end)
        end
        updFov(Config.FOV or 70, true)

        local fovDragging = false
        UI.fovTrack.InputBegan:Connect(function(i)
            if i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                _G.SliderDragging = true
                fovDragging = true
                updFov(fovMIN + ((i.Position.X - UI.fovTrack.AbsolutePosition.X) / UI.fovTrack.AbsoluteSize.X) * (fovMAX - fovMIN), true)
            end
        end)
        UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(i)
            if i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then 
                if fovDragging then SaveConfig() end
                fovDragging = false 
                _G.SliderDragging = false
            end
        end)
        UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(i)
            if fovDragging and (i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
                updFov(fovMIN + ((i.Position.X - UI.fovTrack.AbsolutePosition.X) / UI.fovTrack.AbsoluteSize.X) * (fovMAX - fovMIN), true)
            end
        end)
        UI.fovReset.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() updFov(70) end)

        UI.speedLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", UI.panel)
        UI.speedLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 80, 0, 20); UI.speedLabel.Position = UDim2.new(1, -90, 0, 10)
        UI.speedLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1; UI.speedLabel.Text = "Speed (V)"; UI.speedLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; UI.speedLabel.TextSize = 12; UI.speedLabel.TextColor3 = UI.T.TextPrimary; UI.speedLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right

        -- ── LEFT GRID ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        UI.leftGrid = Instance.new("Frame", UI.panel)
        UI.leftGrid.Size = UDim2.new(0, 240, 0, 190); UI.leftGrid.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 40); UI.leftGrid.BackgroundTransparency = 1

        local function lBtn(txt, pos, size, configKey, callback)
            local b = Instance.new("TextButton", UI.leftGrid)
            b.Size = size; b.Position = pos; b.BackgroundColor3 = UI.T.BtnBg; b.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; b.TextSize = 13; addCorner(b, 6)
            
            local function update()
                local val
                if type(configKey) == "string" then val = Config[configKey]
                elseif type(configKey) == "function" then val = configKey() end
                
                if val ~= nil then
                    b.Text = txt:gsub(": ON", ""):gsub(": OFF", "") .. (val and ": ON" or ": OFF")
                    b.TextColor3 = val and UI.T.TextOn or UI.T.TextOff
                else
                    b.Text = txt; b.TextColor3 = UI.T.TextPrimary
                end
            end
            
            b.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                if type(configKey) == "string" then
                    Config[configKey] = not Config[configKey]; SaveConfig()
                    if callback then callback(Config[configKey]) end
                elseif type(callback) == "function" then
                    callback()
                end
                update()
            end)
            update()
            return b
        end

        local function makeSpeedBtn(defaultVal, pos, size)
            local b = Instance.new("TextButton", UI.leftGrid)
            b.Size = size; b.Position = pos
            b.BackgroundColor3 = UI.T.BtnBg; b.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; b.TextSize = 13
            addCorner(b, 6)

            -- Carrega valor salvo ou usa o padrão
            local cfgKey = "SpeedBtnVal_" .. tostring(defaultVal)
            local val = (Config[cfgKey] and tonumber(Config[cfgKey])) or defaultVal
            b.Text = tostring(val)
            b.TextColor3 = UI.T.TextPrimary

            -- Clique esquerdo: aplica a velocidade
            b.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                if SharedState.applyStealSpeedValue then
                    SharedState.applyStealSpeedValue(val)
                end
                ShowNotification("STEAL SPEED", "Speed: " .. tostring(val))
            end)

            -- Clique direito: editar o número
            b.MouseButton2Click:Connect(function()
                local oldText = b.Text
                b.Text = "..."
                b.TextColor3 = UI.T.FovRed

                -- Cria input overlay
                local overlay = Instance.new("Frame", UI.panel)
                overlay.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                overlay.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
                overlay.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
                overlay.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
                overlay.BorderSizePixel = 0
                overlay.ZIndex = 10

                local box = Instance.new("TextBox", overlay)
                box.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 36)
                box.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
                box.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)
                box.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 15, 30)
                box.BorderSizePixel = 0
                box.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                box.TextSize = 18
                box.TextColor3 = UI.T.TextPrimary
                box.PlaceholderText = tostring(val)
                box.Text = tostring(val)
                box.ZIndex = 11
                Instance.new("UICorner", box).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
                local bs2 = Instance.new("UIStroke", box)
                bs2.Color = UI.T.RotPurple; bs2.Thickness = 1.5
                box:CaptureFocus()

                local function confirm()
                    local num = tonumber(box.Text)
                    if num then
                        num = math.clamp(math.floor(num + 0.5), 1, 99)
                        val = num
                        Config[cfgKey] = num
                        SaveConfig()
                        b.Text = tostring(num)
                    else
                        b.Text = oldText
                    end
                    b.TextColor3 = UI.T.TextPrimary
                    overlay:Destroy()
                end

                box.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
                    confirm()
                end)
            end)

            return b
        end

        makeSpeedBtn(18, UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0), UDim2.new(0, 115, 0, 35))
        makeSpeedBtn(22, UDim2.new(0, 120, 0, 0), UDim2.new(0, 115, 0, 35))
        lBtn("Anti Turret", UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 40), UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 35), "AutoDestroyTurrets", function(v)
            Config.AutoDestroyTurrets = v
            SaveConfig()
        end)
        lBtn("Auto Kick", UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 80), UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 35), "AutoKickOnSteal", function(v)
            -- Controla também o kick do auto pickup
            if _G.AutoPickupKickToggle then _G.AutoPickupKickToggle(v) end
        end)
        lBtn("AB", UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 120), UDim2.new(0, 115, 0, 30), "AutoBack", function(v) if v and _G.startAutoBack then _G.startAutoBack() elseif _G.stopAutoBack then _G.stopAutoBack() end end)
        lBtn("AU", UDim2.new(0, 120, 0, 120), UDim2.new(0, 115, 0, 30), "AutoUnlockOnSteal")

        -- Invis Steal Row
        UI.isBtn = lBtn("Invis Steal", UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 155), UDim2.new(0, 150, 0, 35), "InvisibleStealEnabled", function(v) _G.invisibleStealEnabled = v; if _G.toggleInvisibleSteal then _G.toggleInvisibleSteal() end end)
        
        local function miniToggle(txt, pos, configKey, callback)
            local b = Instance.new("TextButton", UI.leftGrid)
            b.Size = UDim2.new(0, 26, 0, 35); b.Position = pos
            b.BackgroundColor3 = UI.T.BtnBg; b.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; b.TextSize = 9; addCorner(b, 4)
            
            local function update()
                local val = Config[configKey]
                b.Text = txt
                b.TextColor3 = val and UI.T.TextOn or UI.T.TextOff
            end
            
            b.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                Config[configKey] = not Config[configKey]; SaveConfig()
                if callback then callback(Config[configKey]) end
                update()
            end)
            update()
            return b
        end

        miniToggle("AOS", UDim2.new(0, 155, 0, 155), "AutoInvisDuringSteal", function(v) _G.AutoInvisDuringSteal = v end)
        miniToggle("AF", UDim2.new(0, 183, 0, 155), "AutoFacing")
        miniToggle("B", UDim2.new(0, 211, 0, 155), "AutoBlink")

        -- ── RIGHT GRID (Action Buttons) ──────────────────────────────────────────
        UI.rightGrid = Instance.new("Frame", UI.panel)
        UI.rightGrid.Size = UDim2.new(0, 150, 0, 200); UI.rightGrid.Position = UDim2.new(1, -160, 0, 40); UI.rightGrid.BackgroundTransparency = 1

        local function rBtn(txt, x, y, configKey, callback, actionColor)
            local b = Instance.new("TextButton", UI.rightGrid)
            b.Size = UDim2.new(0, 72, 0, 28); b.Position = UDim2.new(0, x*76, 0, y*32); b.BackgroundColor3 = UI.T.BtnBg; b.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; b.TextSize = 10; addCorner(b, 5)
            
            local function update()
                local val
                if type(configKey) == "string" then val = Config[configKey]
                elseif type(configKey) == "function" then val = configKey() end
                
                b.Text = txt
                if val ~= nil then
                    b.TextColor3 = val and UI.T.TextOn or UI.T.TextOff
                else
                    b.TextColor3 = actionColor or UI.T.TextPrimary
                end
            end
            
            b.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                if type(configKey) == "string" then
                    Config[configKey] = not Config[configKey]; SaveConfig()
                    if callback then callback(Config[configKey]) end
                elseif type(callback) == "function" then
                    callback()
                end
                update()
            end)
            update()
            return b
        end

        rBtn("Rejoin", 0, 0, nil, function() TeleportService:Teleport(game.PlaceId, LocalPlayer) end, UI.T.RotPurple)
        rBtn("RJ PS", 1, 0, nil, function() TeleportService:Teleport(game.PlaceId, LocalPlayer) end, UI.T.RotPurple)
        rBtn("Bye", 0, 1, "ByeEnabled", function(v) if v then kickPlayer() end end)
        rBtn("GFs", 1, 1, "CleanErrorGUIs")
        rBtn("High", 0, 2, "HighEnabled")
        rBtn("LS", 1, 2, "AutoRecoverLagback")
        rBtn("Auto", 0, 3, "AutoStealSpeed", function(v)
            if _G.AutoPickupTitanzToggle then _G.AutoPickupTitanzToggle(v) end
        end)
        rBtn("IC", 1, 3, "ICEnabled")
        rBtn("Dual", 0, 4, "DualEnabled")
        rBtn("Move", 1, 4, "MoveEnabled")
        rBtn("Hover", 0, 5, "HoverEnabled")
        rBtn("Spam", 1, 5, "SpamEnabled")
        rBtn("AFK", 0, 6, "AFKEnabled")
        rBtn("Desync", 1, 6, "DesyncVisualizer")

        -- ── BOTTOM SLIDERS (Rot & Dep) ───────────────────────────────────────────
        local function bottomSlider(txt, y, color, configKey, minV, maxV, defaultV)
            local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", UI.panel)
            lbl.Size = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 15); lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, y)
            lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1; lbl.Text = txt; lbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; lbl.TextSize = 10; lbl.TextColor3 = color

            local track = Instance.new("Frame", UI.panel)
            track.Size = UDim2.new(0, 150, 0, 4); track.Position = UDim2.new(0, 40, 0, y + 6); track.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50); addCorner(track, 2)

            local fill = Instance.new("Frame", track)
            fill.BackgroundColor3 = color; addCorner(fill, 2)

            local handle = Instance.new("Frame", track)
            handle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10); handle.BackgroundColor3 = color; addCorner(handle, 5)

            local vLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", UI.panel)
            vLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 15); vLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 195, 0, y)
            vLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1; vLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; vLabel.TextSize = 10; vLabel.TextColor3 = color

            local reset = Instance.new("TextButton", UI.panel)
            reset.Size = UDim2.new(0, 14, 0, 14); reset.Position = UDim2.new(0, 225, 0, y + 1)
            reset.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 40); reset.Text = "R"; reset.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; reset.TextSize = 8; reset.TextColor3 = color; addCorner(reset, 3)

            local function update(v)
                v = math.clamp(v, minV, maxV)
                if configKey == "InvisStealAngle" then v = math.floor(v) end
                Config[configKey] = v; SaveConfig()
                if configKey == "InvisStealAngle" then _G.InvisStealAngle = v elseif configKey == "SinkSliderValue" then _G.SinkSliderValue = v end

                vLabel.Text = (configKey == "SinkSliderValue") and string.format("%.2f", v) or tostring(v)
                local pct = (v - minV) / (maxV - minV)
                fill.Size = UDim2.new(pct, 0, 1, 0)
                handle.Position = UDim2.new(pct, -5, 0.5, -5)
            end
            update(Config[configKey] or defaultV)

            local dragging = false
            track.InputBegan:Connect(function(i)
                if i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                    _G.SliderDragging = true
                    dragging = true
                    update(minV + ((i.Position.X - track.AbsolutePosition.X) / track.AbsoluteSize.X) * (maxV - minV))
                end
            end)
            UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(i)
                if i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then 
                    dragging = false 
                    _G.SliderDragging = false
                end
            end)
            UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(i)
                if dragging and (i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or i.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
                    update(minV + ((i.Position.X - track.AbsolutePosition.X) / track.AbsoluteSize.X) * (maxV - minV))
                end
            end)
            reset.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() update(defaultV) end)
        end

        bottomSlider("Rot", 240, UI.T.RotPurple, "InvisStealAngle", 150, 280, 233)
        bottomSlider("Dep", 260, UI.T.DepOrange, "SinkSliderValue", 0.10, 0.80, 0.10)

        _G.MiniActionsUI = {panel = UI.panel, gui = UI.maGui}
        return UI.maGui
    end

    -- ── AUTO BUY SYSTEM ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    local AB = { active = Config.AutoBuyEnabled or false }
    _G.AutoBuyEsteira = AB.active

    do
        -- Destroy any leftover from previous build
        local _oldAB = PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("BullysAutoBuyUI")
        if _oldAB then _oldAB:Destroy() end

        AB.gui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
        AB.gui.Name         = "BullysAutoBuyUI"
        AB.gui.ResetOnSpawn = false
        AB.gui.IgnoreGuiInset = true
        AB.gui.DisplayOrder = 30
        AB.gui.Parent       = PlayerGui

        AB.panel = Instance.new("Frame", AB.gui)
        AB.panel.Name             = "ABPanel"
        AB.panel.Size             = UDim2.new(0, 215, 0, 260)
        local _savedAbPos = Config.Positions and Config.Positions.AutoBuy or {X=0.01, Y=0.35}
        AB.panel.Position         = UDim2.new(_savedAbPos.X, 0, _savedAbPos.Y, 0)
        AB.panel.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.Background
        AB.panel.BackgroundTransparency = 0.31
        AB.panel.BorderSizePixel  = 0
        AB.panel.Visible          = not (Config.HideAutoBuyUI == true)
        Instance.new("UICorner", AB.panel).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
        AB.stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", AB.panel)
        AB.stroke.Color = Theme.Accent1; AB.stroke.Thickness = 1.8; AB.stroke.Transparency = 0.35
        task.defer(function()
            if addRacetrackBorder then addRacetrackBorder(AB.panel, Theme.Accent1, 3.5) end
        end)

        -- Header + drag
        AB.hdr = Instance.new("Frame", AB.panel)
        AB.hdr.Size               = UDim2.new(1,0,0,36)
        AB.hdr.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        MakeDraggable(AB.hdr, AB.panel, "AutoBuy")

        AB.title = Instance.new("TextLabel", AB.hdr)
        AB.title.Size             = UDim2.new(1,-12,1,0)
        AB.title.Position         = UDim2.new(0,12,0,0)
        AB.title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        AB.title.Text             = "AUTO BUY"
        AB.title.Font             = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
        AB.title.TextSize         = 15
        AB.title.TextColor3       = Theme.Accent1
        AB.title.TextXAlignment   = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

        -- Divider
        AB.div = Instance.new("Frame", AB.panel)
        AB.div.Size             = UDim2.new(1,-20,0,1)
        AB.div.Position         = UDim2.new(0,10,0,36)
        AB.div.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.Accent1
        AB.div.BackgroundTransparency = 0.6
        AB.div.BorderSizePixel  = 0

        -- Content list
        AB.content = Instance.new("Frame", AB.panel)
        AB.content.Size             = UDim2.new(1,-16,1,-46)
        AB.content.Position         = UDim2.new(0,8,0,44)
        AB.content.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        AB.layout = Instance.new("UIListLayout", AB.content)
        AB.layout.Padding   = UDim.new(0,6)
        AB.layout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder

        local function makeAbRow(h, order)
            local r = Instance.new("Frame", AB.content)
            r.Size             = UDim2.new(1,0,0,h)
            r.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.Surface
            r.BackgroundTransparency = 0.05
            r.BorderSizePixel  = 0
            r.LayoutOrder      = order
            Instance.new("UICorner", r).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,7)
            return r
        end

        -- 1) Toggle button
        AB.toggleRow = makeAbRow(38, 1)
        AB.toggleBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", AB.toggleRow)
        AB.toggleBtn.Size             = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
        AB.toggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = AB.active and Theme.Accent1 or Theme.Surface

        AB.toggleBtn.Font             = Enum.Font.GothamBlack

        AB.toggleBtn.BorderSizePixel  = 0
